## Honor Play 10 Overview
### Design and Build
The Honor Play 10 combines simplicity with practicality. It measures 167.7 x 77.7 x 8.6 mm and weighs just 189g, making it comfortable to hold despite its large display. The phone is dust-protected and resistant to water splashes, adding a bit of durability for everyday use.
### Display
The device features a 6.74-inch TFT LCD panel with a 720 x 1600 pixel resolution and a 20:9 aspect ratio. With an 84.2% screen-to-body ratio, it offers a wide viewing experience suited for streaming, browsing, and social media.
### Performance
Running on Android 15 (Go edition), the Honor Play 10 is optimized for lightweight performance and efficiency. It is powered by the MediaTek Helio G81 (12nm) chipset, paired with an octa-core CPU (2x2.0GHz Cortex-A75 & 6x1.7GHz Cortex-A55) and Mali-G52 MC2 GPU, providing reliable performance for daily tasks and light gaming.
### Memory and Storage
The phone comes in two configurations 64GB with 3GB RAM and 128GB with 4GB RAM. It also includes a microSDXC card slot (shared with the SIM tray), allowing for expandable storage to fit your needs.
### Camera System
The Honor Play 10 sports a single 13MP rear camera (f/2.2, wide) with autofocus and LED flash, capable of recording 1080p@30fps videos. On the front, there’s a 5MP selfie camera (f/2.2) that also records in 1080p@30fps, sufficient for video calls and casual selfies.
### Battery and Charging
Fueling the device is a 5000mAh Li-Po battery, designed for long-lasting use. It supports 10W wired charging and reverse wired charging, so you can even power other small devices when needed.
### Connectivity and Features
The Honor Play 10 supports dual 4G LTE, Wi-Fi 5, Bluetooth 5.1, and multiple satellite systems (GPS, GLONASS, GALILEO, BDS) for accurate positioning. It includes FM radio, a USB Type-C 2.0 port with OTG, and a 3.5mm headphone jack, ensuring flexibility in connectivity options.
### Security and Sensors
For quick access, it features a side-mounted fingerprint sensor, along with essential sensors like an accelerometer and proximity sensor to support smart features and gestures.

# Infinix Smart 10: Overview
**Display and Design**
The Infinix Smart 10 packs a big 6.67-inch HD+ LCD screen with a smooth 120Hz refresh rate rare in budget phones sold in Nepal. With 700 nits of brightness, the display stays readable even under sunlight. It has a clean, minimal look with a flat plastic frame and comes in four eye-catching colors like Iris Blue and Twilight Gold. The side-mounted fingerprint sensor and USB-C port keep things practical for daily use.
**Performance and Storage**
Powered by the Unisoc T7250 processor, the Smart 10 handles basic tasks like Facebook, YouTube, and TikTok just fine. It runs on Android 15 with Infinix’s XOS 15.1, which adds some extra custom features. You get 3GB or 4GB RAM, and the software adds another 4GB of virtual RAM for smoother multitasking. Storage options go up to 256GB, and you can even expand it up to 2TB using a microSD card great for Nepali users who love downloading videos or storing files offline.
**Camera and Battery**
The phone has a basic 8MP rear and 8MP front camera—both can shoot up to 2K videos. Don’t expect DSLR-level results, but it’s more than enough for casual photos and video calls. You also get LED flash on both sides for low-light shots. Backing everything is a 5,000mAh battery, which easily lasts a full day on normal use. It supports 15W USB-C charging—faster than the usual 10W in most entry-level phones in Nepal.
**Who It’s For / Ideal Use**
The Infinix Smart 10 is ideal for students, first-time smartphone users, or anyone looking for a solid budget phone in Nepal. It’s perfect for social media, light gaming, streaming, and everyday apps. If you're on a tight budget but still want a large display, good battery life, and decent storage, this phone checks all the right boxes

### Tecno Spark Go 1: Overview 
The Tecno Spark Go 1 is a budget-friendly smartphone that offers a unique blend of design, performance, and essential features. Here’s why it stands out:
#### Stylish Design
The Tecno Spark Go 1 features a flat body with a uniquely shaped camera island that combines elements of both square and circular designs. Available in Glittery White and Startrail Black, the phone offers a stylish and modern look. The Glittery White variant has cloud-like patterns, while the Startrail Black has a grainy texture, adding a touch of personality to your device.
#### Impressive Display
Equipped with a 6.67-inch display, the Spark Go 1 supports a 120Hz refresh rate, ensuring smooth scrolling and fluid animations. The HD+ resolution (720 x 1,600) provides clear and vibrant visuals. A notable feature is the wet and oily touch control, allowing you to use your phone even with water droplets or oil on the screen.
#### Reliable Performance
Powered by the UNISOC T615 processor, the Tecno Spark Go 1 offers balanced performance. This octa-core chipset, with two Cortex-A75 and six Cortex-A55 cores, provides a good balance between power and efficiency. The phone comes with either 3GB or 4GB of RAM, extendable by up to 4GB virtually, making it suitable for multitasking. Storage options include 64GB or 128GB, though there is no option for expansion.
#### Practical Camera Setup
The Tecno Spark Go 1 features a single 13MP rear camera, which is sufficient for everyday photography needs. The front camera is an 8MP unit, perfect for selfies and video calls. Additionally, the second cutout on the back houses an IR blaster, allowing you to control other appliances in your home, adding a practical and convenient feature.
#### Long-Lasting Battery
The phone is equipped with a 5,000mAh battery, supporting 15W fast charging. Tecno claims that the Spark Go 1 can go from 0 to 80% charge in under 90 minutes, ensuring you have plenty of power to get through the day.
#### Connectivity and Security
The Tecno Spark Go 1 offers 4.5G (LTE Advanced) cellular connectivity, ensuring fast and reliable internet access. It also supports WiFi, Bluetooth, and USB Type-C for seamless connectivity. Security features include a side-mounted fingerprint sensor and face unlock, providing quick and convenient access to your device.
#### Affordable and Feature-Rich
Priced competitively, the Tecno Spark Go 1 offers a lot of value for money. Its combination of a stylish design, smooth display, balanced performance, and practical features makes it a standout choice in its segment.
In summary, the Tecno Spark Go 1 is a budget-friendly smartphone that offers a stylish design, smooth display, balanced performance, and practical features. Its standout features, such as the 120Hz refresh rate display, IR blaster, and long-lasting battery, make it a compelling choice for those looking for a reliable and feature-rich phone without breaking the bank.

# Infinix Smart 10 Plus: Overview
**Display and Design**
The Infinix Smart 10 comes with a big 6.67-inch IPS LCD screen that refreshes at 120Hz making scrolling and animations feel super smooth. With a peak brightness of 700 nits, the display stays readable even outdoors. The phone has a simple yet sturdy design with a plastic build and flat edges. It’s IP64 rated for splash resistance and even drop-tested up to 1.5 meters, which is a plus for rough handling especially useful in places like Nepal where phones often go through tough conditions.
**Performance and Storage**
Under the hood, it’s powered by the Unisoc T7250 chipset paired with either 4GB or 8GB RAM. For regular use like YouTube, TikTok, Facebook, or online classes the phone holds up quite well. You get 128GB of internal storage, and there’s a dedicated SD card slot too, which is great for Nepali users who store a lot of videos, songs, or offline content. The device runs on Android 15 with XOS 15.1, which brings some clean and customizable UI features.
**Camera and Battery**
Both the rear and front cameras are 8MP and can shoot up to 2K videos. You won’t get ultra-wide or depth sensors, but for basic photography and selfies, it does the job. It also has dual-LED flash support, helpful during night shots or power cuts. The standout feature here is the massive 6,000mAh battery, which can easily last a day and a half with normal usage. Plus, it supports 18W fast charging and even reverse wired charging, so you can juice up other phones or accessories something very handy when traveling in Nepal.
**Who It’s For / Ideal Use**
The Infinix Smart 10 is perfect for students, budget-conscious users, or anyone looking for a reliable everyday phone in Nepal. It’s ideal for social media, video calls, online learning, and even a bit of entertainment thanks to its big screen and stereo speakers. If you want a phone that lasts long, handles day-to-day use well, and doesn’t cost a fortune, this one hits the sweet spot.

## Realme Note 60x Overview 
### Display and Performance
The Realme Note 60x features a 6.74-inch HD+ IPS LCD screen with a 90Hz refresh rate and 560 nits brightness, ensuring smooth visuals and good visibility even in bright conditions. Powered by a Unisoc T612 processor and 4GB RAM, this phone is well-equipped to handle basic tasks efficiently.
### Camera
The camera setup includes an 8MP rear camera for everyday photography and a 5MP front camera for selfies and video calls. While it may not match the 32MP camera of the Note 60, it still offers decent image quality for casual use.
### Battery and Software
With a 5,000mAh battery and 10W charging, the Realme Note 60x provides long-lasting power to keep you going throughout the day. The device runs on Realme UI based on Android 14, offering a smooth and intuitive user experience.
### Security and Durability
Security is enhanced with a side-mounted fingerprint scanner for quick and secure access. The phone also boasts an IP54 rating, providing protection against dust and water splashes.
### Price in Nepal
The Realme Note 60x is priced at NPR 13,499 for the 4GB/64GB variant, making it an affordable option for those seeking a reliable budget smartphone.
This overview highlights the key features and benefits of the Realme Note 60x, making it an attractive choice for budget-conscious consumers in Nepal.

## Realme Narzo N61 Overview
### Design and Display
The Realme Narzo N61 is basically the same phone as the Realme C61. This reigns true in terms of design and even their promotional materials. But that is a good thing though, because this phone also features Realme’s ArmorShell protection. It is a combination of multiple things like metal build and frame, reinforced glass, coated protection film, shock-absorbing internals, silicone strips and foams, etc. All this adds to the durability of the phone and as a result, it is TÜV Rheinland certified for high reliability. It also comes with IP54 water and dust resistance.
On the front, the phone has a 6.74-inch display with HD+ resolution. The company shies away from mentioning the panel type of the Realme Narzo N61. This leads us to believe that it is a TFT LCD, which is a cheaper panel option commonly seen in this price range. Other than that, the screen is capable of a 90Hz refresh rate, a 180Hz touch sampling rate, and a peak brightness of up to 560 nits.
### Performance and Software
The primary driver on the Realme Narzo N61 is the UNISOC T612 chipset. It is a relatively low-powered silicon that comes in a 12nm fabrication. Furthermore, the processor has eight cores, clocks in at 1.8 GHz, and scores over 250,000 on AnTuTu. Meanwhile, the phone is available in two configurations: 4GB + 64GB, and 6GB + 128GB. It also allows you to expand the memory and storage by up to 6GB and 2TB via software and MicroSD card respectively.
In terms of software, the phone boots on the Realme UI based on Android 14. The company ensures that it will offer a lag-free experience for four years. The Realme Narzo N61 also comes with AI Boost Engine that smoothens the performance and improves the frame rate during demanding activities like gaming and multitasking. It also comes with Mini Capsule 2.0 which is Apple’s Dynamic Island knock-off and Rainwater Smart Touch that improves touch recognition even when your hands or screen is wet.
### Camera and the rest
Optics-wise, you get a 32MP primary shooter and a 5MP selfie camera. There is also an auxiliary lens on the back. However, its purpose has not been stated. It is likely a dummy unit just for show. In the tank, the Realme Narzo N61 packs a 5,000 mAh battery that supports moderate 10W charging. For wireless connectivity, it has dual SIM, 4G LTE, dual-band WiFi, and Bluetooth v5.0. On the other hand, for wired connections, the phone has a USB Type-C port as well as a 3.5mm headphone jack.

## Honor X5b Plus Overview
### Display
The Honor X5b Plus both feature a 6.56-inch TFT LCD display with a resolution of 720 x 1612 pixels. They also share a 90Hz refresh rate and 530 nits peak brightness. The screen-to-body ratio is at around 83.2%.
### Performance
It runs on Android 14 with Magic OS 8. They are powered by the MediaTek Helio G36 chipset, paired with an octa-core CPU (4×2.2 GHz Cortex-A53 & 4×1.6 GHz Cortex-A53). The X5b Plus offer the decent performance capabilities, with the X5b Plus offers 128GB of storage with the 4GB RAM.
### Camera
The X5b Plus steps up with a 50 MP main camera. It features a 5 MP selfie camera with 1080p video recording.
### Battery and Charging
The battery capacity is, 5200 mAh Li-Po battery. It supports 10W wired charging. In terms of connectivity, it offers Wi-Fi 802.11 a/b/g/n/ac, Bluetooth 5.1, and GPS support. They also come with USB Type-C 2.0 and a side-mounted fingerprint sensor.

## Vivo Y19s Overview
The Vivo Y19s is a budget-friendly smartphone that offers a decent blend of performance and features. Powered by a capable processor and backed by ample RAM and storage, it delivers smooth multitasking and ample space for apps and media. The device boasts a vibrant display that brings content to life, while the long-lasting battery ensures you stay connected throughout the day. The Y19s also captures impressive photos and videos, thanks to its versatile camera setup.
### Design and Display
It is more accurate to refer to it as a follow-up to the Y17s, despite the name giving the impression that it is associated with the Y19. Therefore, in terms of design, the phone is sleek, with rounded corners, and seems to have a matte or slightly shimmering finish. Additionally, the phone features two rear cameras that are positioned vertically in an oval-shaped camera module.
This smartphone features a 6.68" LCD panel on the front that has a refresh rate of 90 Hz and a maximum brightness of 1000 nits. It also has an IP64 rating, which makes it dust-tight and provides rudimentary water protection, and a drop-resistant design.  

### Performance
The Vivo Y19s' internal components include a Mali-G57 GPU and a Unisoc T612 chipset, which is based on a 12nm technology and has two Cortex-A75 cores and six A55 cores operating at 1.8GHz.
Additionally, this processor comes with 128 GB of eMMC 5.1 storage and up to 6GB of LPDDR4X RAM. The card tray can hold two nano-SIMs and a microSD, which is a plus, even though none of that is particularly intriguing.
For a phone of this small, the Vivo Y19s' remarkable 5,500mAh battery is amazing. The battery charges at a modest 15W, though. It should survive for a long time even after four years of use if you charge it once a day, as it is rated to retain at least 80% of its original capacity after 1,460 cycles.  

### Camera and the rest
Regarding the camera, it has a 50MP sensor on the back. The selfie camera, which has a 5MP resolution, is located inside a punch hole. Additionally, the camera island has an RGB LED ring that may be utilized for notifications or to give some flair to music.
Additionally, FuntouchOS 14, which is based on Android 14, is released with the Vivo Y19s. It has stereo speakers, and the manufacturer says you can turn up the volume to 300 percent in loud settings. This is probably just a marketing ploy. A 3.5mm headphone jack is also located at the bottom of this smartphone.

# Honor X6c : Overview
**Design and Display**
The Honor X6c brings solid durability for its price, boasting a 5-star SGS rating for drop protection. Thanks to its 360° frame and horn-shaped structure, it can survive accidental drops from up to 1.5 meters even on hard marble floors. It also comes with IP64 certification, so it's safe from dust and light splashes, perfect for daily use.You get to pick from three stylish color options Ocean Cyan, Moonlight White, and Midnight Black. The phone has a slim build with curved edges that feel comfortable in hand. It also includes a side fingerprint scanner, a 3.5mm headphone jack, and a handy AI button for quick tools like translation or homework scanning.The 6.61-inch HD+ IPS display offers a smooth 120Hz refresh rate and can hit up to 1,000 nits brightness, which is great for outdoor use. It also supports eye-friendly features like DC dimming and eBook mode.
**Performance, Battery, and Software**
Under the hood, the Honor X6c is powered by the MediaTek Helio G81 Ultra, paired with 6GB or 8GB of RAM. For storage, it comes with either 128GB or 256GB, and you can expand it with a microSD card great for users who download a lot of media or apps.The 5,300 mAh battery easily lasts a full day and more, even with heavy use. It also supports 35W fast charging, so you won’t be stuck near a socket for long. The phone runs on MagicOS 9 based on Android 15, offering smooth performance and useful AI features like Magic Portal for better multitasking and system optimization.
**Camera and Other Features**
The Honor X6c keeps things simple in the camera department. On the back, there's a 50MP main camera paired with a QVGA depth sensor, which works fine for everyday photos. For selfies and video calls, there's a 5MP front camera tucked inside a punch-hole cutout.Extra features include a reliable side-mounted fingerprint scanner, a headphone jack (which is rare these days), and the AI button for smart tools. The IP64 rating adds peace of mind for users who are always on the go.
**Who It’s For / Ideal Use**
The Honor X6c is ideal for students, casual users, and anyone looking for the best budget phone in Nepal with long battery life and decent daily performance. It's perfect for folks who want a tough phone without spending too much, especially those who rely on basic apps, media, and casual gaming. If you're upgrading from an older entry-level device, this could be a solid step up without breaking the bank.

## HMD Crest: A Versatile Mid-Range Smartphone for 2024
### Design and Display
The HMD Crest brings a sleek and modern design with a focus on durability and functionality. Sporting a well-constructed body, the device features dimensions of 163.9 x 76.4 x 8.4 mm and a solid weight of 205g, making it comfortable to hold while still feeling premium. The standout feature of the Crest is its large 6.67-inch OLED display, offering a crisp 1080 x 2400 pixel resolution with a 20:9 aspect ratio. The vibrant OLED panel provides deep blacks, excellent contrast, and sharp details, while the high screen-to-body ratio ensures an immersive viewing experience. With the added benefit of a 395 ppi density, the Crest excels at media consumption, making it a great option for those who enjoy watching videos or playing games on their device.
### Performance
Powering the HMD Crest is the Unisoc T760 chipset, built on a 6nm process, and paired with an octa-core CPU configuration (1x Cortex-A76 at 2.2GHz, 3x Cortex-A76, and 4x Cortex-A55). This setup delivers smooth performance across most day-to-day tasks, such as browsing, social media, and gaming. The device is equipped with 6GB of RAM, making multitasking seamless and efficient. For internal storage, users get 128GB, which can be expanded via the microSD slot (using a shared SIM slot), offering flexibility for those who need extra space for apps and media.
Running on Android 14, the device provides a clean and responsive user interface, optimized for performance and ease of use. The Mali-G57 GPU ensures decent graphics rendering, making the device capable of handling casual gaming and media playback with ease.
### Camera
The HMD Crest is equipped with a dual-camera setup, featuring a 50MP wide-angle primary sensor that delivers clear, detailed photos in most lighting conditions, supported by a 2MP depth sensor for bokeh effects in portrait shots. The camera system includes features like LED flash and HDR, enhancing the photo quality in diverse environments. The rear camera setup is capable of recording 1080p videos at 30fps, providing solid video quality for daily use. On the front, a 50MP selfie camera ensures sharp and vibrant self-portraits, supported by video capabilities, making it perfect for video calls or content creation.
### Battery, Charging, and Connectivity
The HMD Crest houses a 5000mAh battery that promises all-day usage on a single charge. For those who need a quick power top-up, it supports 33W wired fast charging, ensuring that the device can be charged up quickly when necessary. The device’s connectivity suite includes 5G support, allowing for high-speed data transfer where available, as well as 4G LTE, Wi-Fi 802.11 a/b/g/n/ac, Bluetooth 5.0, and USB Type-C for fast data transfer and charging. The Crest also includes a 3.5mm headphone jack, which is becoming rare in many modern devices, making it a plus for users who prefer wired audio.
In terms of positioning, the HMD Crest includes GPS and GALILEO for accurate location tracking, although it lacks NFC support, which may be a dealbreaker for some users who rely on contactless payments.
### Durability and Repairability
A key feature of the HMD Crest is its focus on durability and repairability. It is dust and splash resistant, ensuring it can handle minor exposure to water and dust. The device is also repair-it-yourself capable, allowing users to easily replace key components like the display, back cover, battery, and charging port. This adds a layer of longevity to the device, allowing users to maintain and fix the phone without needing to go to a service center.

## Redmi 14C Overview
The Xiaomi Redmi 14C is a remarkable smartphone that offers exceptional value without compromising on performance. With its stylish design, powerful features, and affordable price, this device is perfect for those seeking a reliable and efficient companion.
### Design and Display
This phone, which is the Redmi 13C's replacement, has a very different appearance. Instead of a squircle camera island on the side, we have a huge circular one aligned at the center. In Nepal, the color options are Midnight Black, Sage Green, and Dreamy Purple.  
  
The Redmi 14C's 6.88-inch screen has expanded significantly in size. Even though it's enormous, the display is only average in quality. Only HD+ resolution and 8-bit color with 70% NTSC gamut coverage are available. This device has a maximum brightness of 600 nits. It does, however, have a touch sampling rate of 240 Hz and a smooth refresh rate of 120 Hz.
### Performance
The Redmi 14C was intended to come with the MediaTek Helio G91 Ultra, according to the leak. But instead, the Helio G81 Ultra phone has arrived. It is a new chipset that seems to be an improvement over the 2020 G80 processor. It might have used a more recent fabrication technique, even if the peak frequency and core architecture seem to have remained the same.
Meanwhile, there are three alternative configurations available for this phone. 4GB + 128GB, 6GB + 128GB, and 8GB + 256GB are those. Here, the storage is eMMC 5.1 and the RAM is LPDDR4X. Up to 8GB of additional memory can be added to this phone. Storage expansion is also an option, however it's unclear how much it can hold.
### Camera and the rest
It appears that the phone has four cameras, but this is untrue. Not even any lenses are housed in two of the back cutouts. One serves as an LED flash, and the other is utilized to brand the "50MP AI Camera." Yes, a 50MP main sensor is included with the Redmi 14C. Even the firm dismisses another lens by calling it a "auxiliary lens." As a result, this phone essentially has a single camera. A 13MP camera for selfies and face unlock is located on the front.
Regarding the battery, the Redmi 14C has a 5,160 mAh cell and is capable of 18W rapid charging via a USB Type-C connector. For further protection, a fingerprint sensor is built inside the power button.

# Infinix Hot 50 Pro Price in Nepal: Stylish Design Meets High-End Display
The Infinix Hot 50 Pro stands out in Nepal’s mid-range smartphone market with its sleek, modern design and premium display features. Sharing its design DNA with the rest of the Hot 50 series, the phone features flat edges, a clean back panel, and unique squircle-shaped camera modules that give it a distinct look. The device also comes with IP54 rating, making it resistant to dust and splashes — a rare bonus at this price point. Infinix is offering three color variants, including a sleek Titanium Grey. Up front, the 6.78-inch AMOLED screen boasts FHD+ resolution and an adaptive refresh rate of up to 120Hz. Whether you're scrolling social media or gaming, the 1,800 nits peak brightness, 1,500Hz touch sampling rate, and full DCI-P3 color gamut.
**Powerful Performance with Gaming in Mind**
Under the hood, the Infinix Hot 50 Pro in Nepal runs on the MediaTek Helio G100 chipset, built on a power-efficient 6nm process. With a peak clock speed of 2.2GHz, the phone is paired with up to 8GB RAM and 256GB of storage — expandable via a microSD slot up to 2TB. The device supports Dynamic RAM Expansion, effectively giving you more multitasking power. This setup ensures smooth performance for casual users and mobile gamers alike. Infinix has optimized the phone for games like FreeFire and Mobile Legends, offering up to 90FPS gameplay. Backing it all is a large 5,000mAh battery with 33W fast charging. Battery features like bypass charging, liquid detection, and overnight protection further enhance longevity — ideal for users in Nepal who need all-day battery on the go.
**Camera and AI Features Tailored for Daily Use**
For photography lovers, the Infinix Hot 50 Pro price in Nepal delivers solid camera hardware for the budget. The main 50MP rear camera, powered by the Hi-5022Q sensor, captures clear daylight shots with good detail. There’s also a secondary 2MP sensor, primarily for depth, though Infinix hasn’t detailed it fully. On the front, the 8MP selfie camera uses the GC08A8 sensor and is backed by Infinix AI for improved skin tones and lighting. Whether you’re snapping portraits or shooting TikToks, the AI enhancements help balance colors and contrast well. All in all, the Hot 50 Pro is a value-packed smartphone that balances design, performance, and display — making it a strong contender in Nepal’s competitive mobile space.

## Vivo Y19s Pro 
The vivo Y19s Pro is designed for users who want lasting performance without breaking the bank. Running on Android 15 and powered by the UNISOC T612 chipset, it handles everyday tasks smoothly whether it's social media, browsing, or light gaming.
### Display & Design
Its 6.68-inch LCD screen delivers a 90Hz refresh rate for smoother scrolling and visuals. With 1000 nits peak brightness, it stays visible even in sunlight. The phone feels solid in hand, with a slim 8.1mm profile and a side-mounted fingerprint sensor for quick access.
### Performance & Storage
You get up to 8GB RAM, expandable by another 8GB, keeping multitasking fluid. Storage isn’t a concern either, with 128GB built-in and support for up to 1TB via microSD.
### Camera Experience
The 50MP rear camera captures bright, detailed shots during the day, while dedicated modes like Night, Portrait, and Pro help tailor your photos. On the front, a 5MP selfie camera covers the basics well.
### Battery & Charging
Its massive 6000mAh battery easily lasts a full day and more, and when it’s time to charge, the 44W fast charging gets you back up quickly.
### Connectivity & Features
You get dual-band Wi-Fi, Bluetooth 5.2, GPS, FM radio, USB-C, and even a 3-card slot setup 2 SIMs and a microSD without compromises.

## Realme C63 Overview
### Design and Display
The Realme C63 features a design reminiscent of iPhones, with a squircle camera island housing three circular cutouts. The back panel is available in two unique finishes: Leather Blue, which offers a vegan leather texture, and Jade Green, featuring a smooth surface with watery patterns. The phone is also IP54-rated for dust and water resistance, ensuring durability against accidental splashes and dust ingress.
On the front, the Realme C63 sports a 6.74-inch display with a waterdrop notch. The display supports a 90Hz refresh rate and a 180Hz touch sampling rate, providing smooth visuals and responsive touch interactions. It offers an HD+ resolution and a brightness range from 1 nit to 560 nits, making it suitable for various lighting conditions.
### Performance
Powered by the UNISOC T612 processor, the Realme C63 delivers reliable performance for everyday tasks. This octa-core chipset, fabricated on a 12nm process, clocks in at 1.8GHz. The phone is available in two RAM configurations—6GB and 8GB—with the option to extend RAM virtually by an additional 8GB. Storage options include 128GB and 256GB, with support for external storage via a microSD card.
### Camera and Battery
The Realme C63 is equipped with a 50MP primary camera, capable of standard functions and QR code scanning. The auxiliary lens serves primarily as a decorative element. On the front, an 8MP camera supports features like Air Gesture, allowing users to perform tasks such as scrolling by waving in front of the screen.
The phone packs a 5,000 mAh battery with 45W fast charging support, ensuring quick recharges and long-lasting usage. Additionally, the Realme C63 includes features like Mini Capsule 2.0, a dynamic notification interface inspired by Apple’s Dynamic Island, and customizable power button functions, similar to the iPhone 15 series’ Action button.
### Software and Additional Features
The Realme C63 comes with several software enhancements, including AI Boost for optimized gaming and multitasking performance. The phone also supports 360° NFC, adding convenience for contactless payments and data transfers. Realme's optimizations ensure that the C63 meets the 48-month Fluency Certification, promising smooth performance over extended use.
Overall, the Realme C63 offers a compelling package with its stylish design, reliable performance, and innovative features, making it an attractive choice for budget-conscious consumers seeking a feature-rich smartphone.

### Tecno Spark 30 : Overview 
The Tecno Spark 30 is a compelling choice for those seeking a reliable smartphone with standout features at an affordable price. Here’s why it shines:
#### Exceptional Display
The Tecno Spark 30 boasts a 6.78-inch LCD display with a 90Hz refresh rate, ensuring smooth scrolling and fluid animations. Its FHD+ resolution (1,080 x 2,460) and 800 nits peak brightness make visuals crisp and vibrant, even in bright sunlight. A unique feature is the wet and oily touch control, perfect for those who often use their phones in less-than-ideal conditions.
#### Powerful Performance
Powered by the MediaTek Helio G91 chipset, the Spark 30 offers robust performance. This octa-core processor, combined with 8GB of RAM (extendable by another 8GB virtually), ensures smooth multitasking and gaming experiences. The phone also comes with generous storage options of 128GB or 256GB, giving users plenty of space for apps, photos, and videos.
#### High-Quality Camera
The standout feature of the Tecno Spark 30 is its 64MP primary camera with a Sony IMX682 sensor. This setup delivers stunning photos with excellent detail and clarity. The 13MP front camera, equipped with a dual-color temperature flash, ensures great selfies even in low light. The absence of auxiliary lenses means the main camera handles all photography tasks, making it versatile and reliable.
#### Enhanced Audio and Media Experience
The Spark 30 features a stereo speaker setup with Dolby Atmos audio, providing an immersive and rich sound experience. Whether you’re watching videos or listening to music, the enhanced audio quality makes media consumption a delight.
#### Long-Lasting Battery
Equipped with a 5,000mAh battery, the Tecno Spark 30 offers long-lasting power, making it ideal for heavy users. The 18W wired charging support ensures quick recharging, so you can get back to using your phone in no time.
#### Durability and Connectivity
The phone’s IP64 rating provides higher dust resistance, making it more durable. It also supports NFC and an IR blaster, adding to its versatility. The connectivity options include 4G cellular, WiFi 5, and Bluetooth v5.0, ensuring you stay connected.
#### Affordable and Feature-Rich
Priced competitively, the Tecno Spark 30 offers a lot of value for money. Its combination of a high-quality display, powerful performance, excellent camera, and long-lasting battery makes it a standout choice in its segment.
In summary, the Tecno Spark 30 is a feature-packed smartphone that offers a blend of performance, display quality, and camera capabilities at an affordable price. Its standout features, such as the high-refresh-rate display, powerful chipset, and high-quality camera, make it a compelling choice for anyone looking for a reliable and feature-rich phone.

# HMD Crest Max Overview: A Mid-Range Powerhouse for Nepalese Users
**Power Meets Efficiency:**
The HMD Crest Max emerges as a compelling mid-range smartphone in Nepal’s fast-growing Android market, offering solid specs at a competitive price. Engineered for both performance and sustainability, it sports a sleek 6.67-inch OLED display with Full HD+ resolution (1080 x 2400 pixels), offering vibrant visuals and sharp content—ideal for streaming, gaming, and social media. With Android 14 out of the box, the Crest Max provides a clean software experience and is powered by the Unisoc T760 chipset, built on a 6nm process. This octa-core processor, combined with 8GB RAM and 256GB storage, makes multitasking smooth, while a microSDXC slot offers storage expansion (shared SIM slot).
**Built for Nepal: Repairable Design, 5G Support, and Long-Lasting Battery Life:**
One of the standout features for the Nepalese market is its repair-it-yourself capability a rare offering in this segment. Users can replace the battery, back cover, display, and even the charging port on their own, making it a sustainable choice for those in remote areas or looking to save on repair costs. The 5000 mAh battery, which is also user-replaceable, ensures full-day usage with ease, while 33W fast charging adds convenience. The phone supports 5G connectivity in Nepal with bands 1, 3, 28, 40, and 78, making it future-ready for networks being rolled out across major cities. Add to that dual nano-SIM slots, side-mounted fingerprint sensor, and IP-rated splash and dust resistance, and you have a device ready for the diverse conditions of Nepal.
**Camera-Centric Experience with 50MP Selfie Shooter and Reliable Daily Performance:**
Camera-wise, the 64MP main shooter is capable enough for day-to-day photography, complemented by a 5MP ultrawide and a 2MP macro sensor. The real surprise is the 50MP front camera, which caters well to selfie lovers and content creators on TikTok, Instagram, and YouTube—platforms growing rapidly in Nepal. Despite lacking NFC, the Crest Max covers all essentials with Wi-Fi ac, Bluetooth 5.0, and USB Type-C support. The inclusion of a 3.5mm headphone jack is another win for users who still prefer wired audio. Plus, the “Deep Purple” colorway adds a touch of style to an otherwise functional design.
**Conclusion:**
The HMD Crest Max is a well-rounded mid-range 5G smartphone with practical features, sustainable design, and solid performance, perfectly aligned with the needs of modern smartphone users in Nepal.

### Moto G45 5G: A Budget Phone That Delivers
The Moto G45 5G is a stylish and affordable smartphone packed with useful features. It comes in three eye-catching colors—Brilliant Blue, Brilliant Green, and Viva Magenta—all with a soft, leather-like back. It’s also water-repellent and has Gorilla Glass protection, making it durable for everyday life.
The phone has a 6.5-inch bright display that’s great for watching videos or scrolling through social media. It’s smooth to use, thanks to a refresh rate that adjusts up to 120Hz for fast and fluid visuals.
Under the hood, it’s powered by the Snapdragon 6s Gen 3 processor, which makes the phone quick and reliable for gaming, streaming, or multitasking. It comes with 4GB or 8GB of RAM, and you can expand it virtually for even better performance. Plus, the 128GB of storage ensures you have plenty of room for your photos, apps, and videos.
The camera setup includes a 50MP main camera for sharp photos and a 16MP front camera for selfies. While it doesn’t have an ultrawide lens, it does include a depth sensor for portrait shots. A 5,000mAh battery keeps the phone running all day, and it charges quickly with its USB-C port.
It runs on the latest Android 14, and Motorola promises updates to keep the phone secure and up-to-date.
### Why It’s a Great Buy:
  * **Stylish and durable design** with water-repellent features.
  * **Bright and smooth display** for a great viewing experience.
  * **Fast performance** with a reliable processor and 5G support.
  * **Great cameras** for high-quality photos and selfies.
  * **Long-lasting battery** for all-day use.

# Vivo Y29 Overview
Vivo has consistently aimed to deliver a blend of robust performance and innovative design with its Y-series smartphones. The Vivo Y29 is no exception, offering a comprehensive package that caters to a wide range of users. From its durable design to its impressive camera capabilities, the Y29 stands out as a reliable choice in the mid-range segment. Let's delve into the key features of this device.
#### Design and Display
The Vivo Y29 boasts a design that mirrors its 5G counterpart, ensuring a familiar and polished aesthetic. A notable addition is the Aura light situated just below the camera module, enhancing low-light portrait photography with a subtle glow. For added durability, the Y29 features an Anti-Drop armor design, providing extra sturdiness to withstand accidental drops.
On the display front, the Y29 is equipped with a 6.68-inch LCD screen that offers a 120Hz refresh rate. This high refresh rate ensures smooth scrolling and fluid animations, making it ideal for gaming and media consumption. The display also peaks at 1,000 nits of brightness, ensuring clear visibility even in bright conditions. With a pixel density of 264 ppi, the screen delivers sharp and detailed visuals, perfect for enjoying various types of media.
#### Performance and Software
Under the hood, the Vivo Y29 is powered by the Snapdragon 685 SoC, a chip announced in December 2020. While it may be a few years old, it still delivers reliable performance for everyday tasks. The device runs on Android 15, customized with Vivo's Funtouch OS 15, offering a user-friendly interface with a range of customization options.
The Y29 offers up to 6GB or 8GB of RAM, providing ample memory for multitasking and running multiple apps simultaneously. Storage options include 128GB or 256GB, giving users the flexibility to store a large number of apps, photos, and videos. The combination of a capable processor and sufficient RAM ensures that the Vivo Y29 can handle most tasks with ease, making it a solid choice for both casual users and those with more demanding needs.
#### Camera Setup
The Vivo Y29 features an 8MP front camera housed in a centered punch-hole, perfect for taking clear and detailed selfies. On the rear, the phone boasts a 50MP primary camera, capable of capturing high-resolution photos with impressive detail. Accompanying the primary camera is a 2MP secondary sensor, which adds versatility to the camera setup.
In addition to the camera hardware, the Y29 includes a flash and a ring light. The ring light serves dual purposes: it enhances low-light photography and acts as a notification indicator for calls, messages, and music playback. This thoughtful inclusion adds a touch of convenience and style to the overall camera experience.
#### Battery and Charging
One of the standout features of the Vivo Y29 is its substantial 6,500mAh battery. This large capacity ensures extended usage time, allowing users to go through a full day of heavy use without worrying about running out of power. To complement the large battery, the Y29 supports 44W fast charging, enabling quick power-ups and reducing downtime.
The device also supports 4G connectivity, including VoLTE (Voice over LTE) for NTC and Ncell networks, ensuring clear and reliable voice calls. Additionally, it features VoWiFi (Voice over WiFi) support for NTC, allowing users to make voice calls over WiFi when cellular coverage is weak. For added security and convenience, the Y29 includes a side-mounted fingerprint scanner, providing quick and easy access to the device.
### Conclusion
The Vivo Y29 is a well-rounded smartphone that offers a blend of durability, performance, and impressive camera capabilities. Its Anti-Drop armor design and Aura light add unique touches to the overall user experience. The 6.68-inch LCD display with a 120Hz refresh rate ensures smooth visuals and vibrant colors, making it perfect for media consumption. Powered by the Snapdragon 685 SoC and running on Android 15 with Funtouch OS 15, the Y29 delivers reliable performance and a user-friendly interface.
With a 50MP primary camera and an 8MP front camera, the Y29 is equipped to capture stunning photos and selfies. The inclusion of a ring light for notifications and low-light photography adds a practical and stylish touch. The large 6,500mAh battery and 44W fast charging capability ensure that users can enjoy extended usage without frequent recharges.
Overall, the Vivo Y29 is a strong contender in the mid-range market, offering a comprehensive package that caters to a wide range of users. Whether you're looking for a durable phone with a great camera or a device that can handle your daily tasks with ease, the Vivo Y29 is definitely worth considering.

## Samsung Galaxy M16 5G Overview
### Design and Display
The Samsung Galaxy M16 features a more modern design with sharper, flatter edges, moving away from the rounded contours seen on the M15. It is available in three color options: Blush Pink, Mint Green, and Thunder Black. On the back, a vertically aligned pill-shaped camera module houses multiple sensors, accompanied by an LED flash unit placed outside the camera island.
At the front, the device sports a 6.7-inch AMOLED display with thin bezels, though the bottom chin appears slightly thicker than the sides. Meanwhile, the notorious U-shaped notch from 8 years back is still here to stay. Other than that, the screen offers FHD+ resolution, 90Hz refresh rate, and up to 800 nits of HBM, making it ideal for media consumption and outdoor visibility.
### Performance and Storage
Under the hood, the Galaxy M16 runs on the MediaTek Dimensity 6300 SoC, featuring two high-performance Cortex-A76 cores (clocked at 2.4 GHz) and six power-efficient Cortex-A55 cores (clocked at 2.0 GHz). For graphics, it is equipped with the Arm Mali-G57 MC2 GPU.
The device comes with up to 8GB of RAM and 128GB of internal storage, expandable via a microSD card slot (up to 1TB). Samsung also offers virtual RAM expansion. Meanwhile, this phone boots on One UI 7 out of the box, bringing new customization options, improved battery optimizations, and enhanced privacy features. and will get 6 years of OS and security updates.
### Camera
The Galaxy M16 features a 50MP primary camera with an f/1.8 aperture. Accompanying it is a 5MP ultra-wide sensor and a 2MP macro sensor. For selfies, the 13MP front camera with an f/2.0 aperture ensures sharp and vibrant self-portraits as per Samsung, along with Face Unlock support for added security.
### Connectivity and Rest
The Galaxy M16 supports dual-band 5GHz Wi-Fi, and 5G support for faster network speeds and lower latency. The device ships with Android 15 out of the box, running Samsung’s One UI 7 interface, which brings new customization features, improved security, and enhanced battery optimization.
Additionally, the Galaxy M16 packs a 5000mAh battery. It also supports 25W fast charging for quick top-ups. Other features include stereo speakers, and a fingerprint scanner.

### Redmi Note 14 4G: Overview
#### Design and Display
The Redmi Note 14 4G adopts a similar design language as its 5G sibling, featuring a square camera module, a curved middle frame, and a curved display upfront. It carries an IP54 rating, offering protection against dust and water splashes.  
The smartphone boasts a 6.67-inch AMOLED display with an FHD+ resolution, a 120Hz refresh rate, a peak brightness of 1800 nits, and Gorilla Glass 5 for durability. It comes in four stylish color options: Ocean Blue, Midnight Black, Mist Purple, and Lime Green.
#### Performance
Powered by the Mediatek Helio G99 Ultra chipset, the Redmi Note 14 4G delivers modest performance upgrades over its predecessor's Helio G99. Built on a 6nm process, it is coupled with 6GB or 8GB of LPDDR4X RAM and storage options of 128GB, 256GB, or 512GB.  
On the software front, it runs Xiaomi HyperOS, based on Android 14.
#### Cameras
The phone retains the same camera setup as its predecessor, including:
  * A 108 MP primary sensor with Optical Image Stabilization (OIS)
  * A 2MP macro sensor


It also supports AI-based features such as AI Erase Pro and AI Beautify. However, the device is limited to 1080p at 30fps video recording, with no 4K support. For selfies and video calls, a 20 MP front camera is provided.
#### Battery and Charging
The Redmi Note 14 4G packs a large 5500mAh battery with support for 33W fast charging, ensuring all-day usage and quick charging times.
#### Connectivity and Other Features
Key connectivity options include:
  * WiFi 5
  * 4G with VoLTE
  * Bluetooth 5.3
  * NFC
  * USB Type-C port


Other notable features are:
  * An in-display fingerprint scanner for secure access
  * A Dolby-powered dual stereo speaker setup for immersive audio

## Honor X7d 4G Overview
### Design and Build
The Honor X7d 4G comes with a sleek yet durable build, measuring 166.9 x 76.8 x 8.2 mm and weighing 208g. It features an IP65 rating, making it dust-tight and resistant to low-pressure water jets ideal for daily use. Available in Desert Gold, Ocean Cyan, Meteor Silver, and Velvet Black, it combines practicality with style.
### Display
Up front, the phone sports a 6.77-inch TFT LCD display with a 120Hz refresh rate for smoother visuals. The 720 x 1610p resolution and 86% screen-to-body ratio offer an immersive viewing experience. It’s protected by tempered glass (Mohs level 4), ensuring decent scratch resistance.
### Performance
Powered by the Qualcomm Snapdragon 685 (6nm) chipset, the X7d 4G handles daily tasks efficiently. Its octa-core CPU (4x2.8GHz Cortex-A73 + 4x1.9GHz Cortex-A53) and Adreno 610 GPU ensure stable performance for multitasking and casual gaming. It runs on Android 15 with MagicOS 9, offering a modern, smooth interface.
### Memory and Storage
The device comes in multiple configurations 128GB with 6GB or 8GB RAM, and 256GB with 8GB RAM. Although the card slot remains unspecified, the generous internal storage options make it suitable for everyday use and app-heavy users.
### Camera System
On the back, the Honor X7d 4G features a dual-camera setup with a 108MP main sensor (f/1.8, PDAF) and a 2MP depth lens. It supports 1080p video recording at 30fps. For selfies, there’s an 8MP front camera, also capable of 1080p@30fps recording great for social media shots and video calls.
### Battery and Charging
A major highlight is its massive 6500mAh Li-Po battery, promising exceptional endurance rated at 71 hours. With 35W wired charging, it refuels quickly, offering more uptime with less waiting. The battery is rated for 1600 charge cycles, emphasizing long-term durability.
### Connectivity and Features
Connectivity options include dual 4G LTE, Wi-Fi 5, Bluetooth 5.0, GPS, and NFC (region-dependent). The device uses a USB Type-C 2.0 port with OTG support. Security is handled by a side-mounted fingerprint sensor, complemented by accelerometer, proximity, and compass sensors.
### Durability and Efficiency
Honor emphasizes reliability with EU Energy Class A efficiency and Free Fall Class A (270 falls) durability certification. The Repairability Class B rating also suggests the device is easier to maintain than many budget phones.

## Infinix Hot 60 Pro+
### Camera Setup
The Redmi A5 4G sports an 8MP front camera, upgraded from the 5MP in previous models. However, the rear camera has been downgraded to 32MP from the 50MP sensors found in earlier versions.
### Performance
The phone runs on a Unisoc T7250 chipset with 4G connectivity. This processor contains two Cortex-A75 cores at 1.8GHz and six Cortex-A55 cores at 1.6GHz, paired with a Mali-G57 GPU running at 850MHz. Performance-wise, it’s similar to the Helio G81 Ultra in the Redmi A3 Pro but weaker than the Snapdragon 4s Gen 2 found in the Redmi A4.
### Battery
The Redmi A5 4G is powered by a 5,200mAh battery with 18W charging support, though the package includes a 15W adapter.

## Redmi Note 14 5G Overview
### Design and Display
The core design of both phones remains the same, however, the Redmi has given the Note 14 5G enough tweaks to be visually distinguishable. The camera cutout has grown larger, while the back panel has gone back to being curved. Similarly, the camera island has gone a bit softer with the edge and the LED flash has shifted a coupled millimetres up. The phone offers an added level of durability with an IP64 rating, reinforced internal design, and Corning Gorilla Glass 5 protection.
On the front, it has a 6.67-inch OLED screen with FHD+ resolution. It offers a refresh rate of up to 120Hz and a peak brightness of 2,100 nits. You also get a standard and instantaneous touch sampling rate of 240Hz and 2,160Hz respectively. The display is capable of HDR10+ and covers the DCI-P3 color gamut. Moreover, it has received TÜV and SGS certifications for eye care features like low blue light.
### Performance
The MediaTek Dimensity 7025 Ultra serves as the brain of the Redmi Note 14 5G. With 6nm fabrication and a higher 2.5GHz clock speed, this chipset offers a decent upgrade over the Dimensity 6080 on its predecessor. Furthermore, the chip is paired with up to 12 GB of RAM and 512GB of UFS 2.2 storage. However only the 8/128GB and 8/256GB are likely to launch in Nepal For battery, it has a sizable 5,110 mAh cell with 45W charging support.
### Camera and the rest
The primary shooter on the Redmi Note 14 5G is a 108MP OIS-enabled lens coupled with a Sony LYT-600 sensor. Additionally, there is an 8MP ultrawide unit and a 2MP macro sensor. The latter barely adds to the photography experience though. Meanwhile, a 20MP camera sits on the front for selfies and 2D face scanning.
Connectivity-wise, you get dual-SIM support with 5G cellular, dual-band WiFi 5, and Bluetooth v5.3 for wireless medium. On the other hand, a USB Type-C port and a 3.5mm headphone jack handle the wired connections. For additional security, there is an in-display fingerprint sensor. The company also mentions “Heart rate detection” as a feature on this phone, but refuses to elaborate any further.

### Moto G64 5G: Overview
The Moto G64 5G is a solid choice for anyone looking for a budget-friendly smartphone with excellent features. It comes in a sleek and durable design with an IP52 water-repellent body and three eye-catching color options: Mint Green, Pearl Blue, and Ice Lilac. Its 6.5-inch FHD+ display with a smooth 120Hz refresh rate ensures a great viewing experience for videos, browsing, and gaming.
Powered by the MediaTek Dimensity 7025 processor, the Moto G64 5G delivers reliable performance for multitasking and everyday use. You can choose between 8GB or 12GB of RAM and up to 256GB of storage, which can be expanded to 1TB with a microSD card—perfect for those who need extra space for apps, photos, and videos.
The camera setup is versatile, featuring a 50MP main camera with optical image stabilization (OIS) for clear, steady photos and an 8MP ultrawide lens that also works as a macro shooter. The 16MP front camera takes sharp selfies and supports facial recognition for added convenience.
A massive 6,000mAh battery powers the phone, lasting easily through a day or more, and it supports 30W fast charging with a 33W charger included in the box. The Moto G64 5G also features dual speakers for immersive audio and includes a headphone jack for wired audio fans. It supports 5G connectivity, dual-band WiFi, and Bluetooth 5.3, ensuring a smooth and fast connection.
With its excellent display, reliable performance, impressive cameras, and long battery life, the Moto G64 5G offers great value for anyone looking for a capable and affordable 5G smartphone.

# Honor X8c Price in Nepal and Overview
The Honor X8c is an excellent mid-range smartphone now available in Nepal at a starting price of around Rs. 28,000. It combines an attractive design, powerful performance, and premium features, making it a top choice for users seeking a reliable phone under a budget. With multiple variants including 128GB 6GB RAM, 128GB 8GB RAM, 256GB 8GB RAM, and 512GB 8GB RAM, users in Nepal can choose a configuration that best fits their needs and budget. The phone is slim and lightweight, measuring 7.1mm in thickness and weighing just 174g, offering a comfortable grip and a premium in-hand feel.
## Display and Design
The Honor X8c sports a beautiful 6.7-inch AMOLED display with a 120Hz refresh rate, 1080 x 2412 resolution, and a 20:9 aspect ratio. With a peak brightness of 2800 nits, it ensures excellent visibility even in direct sunlight, which is ideal for outdoor usage across various regions of Nepal. The screen delivers vibrant colors and smooth scrolling, making it perfect for gaming, video streaming, and daily use. It boasts an ~89.9% screen-to-body ratio, providing an immersive visual experience. Color options like Marrs Green, Midnight Black, Moonlight White, and Cloud Purple offer a touch of personality and elegance to the device.
## Performance and Battery
Powered by the Snapdragon 685 (6nm) chipset, the Honor X8c runs on Android 15 with MagicOS 9, delivering smooth and efficient performance for multitasking, gaming, and productivity. The Octa-core CPU ensures lag-free usage for most day-to-day tasks. Backing the performance is a robust 5000mAh battery, capable of powering the phone throughout the day—even in areas with limited electricity, making it a reliable companion for users in rural and urban Nepal alike. The device also supports USB Type-C 2.0 with OTG, adding convenience for data sharing and charging.
## Camera and Connectivity Features
The camera setup on the Honor X8c is a major highlight. It features a 108MP main rear camera with OIS, paired with a 5MP ultrawide lens, offering high-quality photography. The front houses a sharp 50MP selfie camera, making it great for selfies, video calls, and vlogging. Both cameras support 1080p video recording at 30fps with gyro-EIS, ensuring smooth and stable footage. Connectivity features include dual Nano-SIM, Bluetooth 5.0/5.1, Wi-Fi, GPS, and a side-mounted fingerprint sensor. With sensors like gyro, compass, and ultrasonic proximity, the Honor X8c is a full-featured smartphone perfect for the Nepali market.

## CMF Phone 1 Overview
### Design and Display
Let’s address the most important side of the CMF Phone 1, which is its design. What sets this guy apart from the usual boring midrange phone is its interchangeable back cover. You can just simply open the screws for that. On the bottom, there is a rotating dial that acts as an accessory holder. Nothing ships this phone in two shades: Black, and Light Green in Nepal.
Flipping to the front, the phone houses a 6.67-inch AMOLED panel with a 120Hz refresh rate. It is HDR 10+ certified and boasts a 2000nits of peak brightness.
### Performance
Powering the things from the core is a new Dimensity 7300 SoC. This 4nm-based 5G chipset is however less powerful than the Dimensity 7200 chip. Yes, you heard that right because this new chip features less powerful Cortex-A78 and Cortex-A55 cores as compared to the 7200’s more powerful Cortex-A715 cores and Cortex-A510 cores. Handling the graphics here is a Mali-G615 MC2 GPU.
CMF has paired the processor with 8GB of RAM and 128/256GB of UFS 2.2 internal storage. Meanwhile, booting the Phone 1 is Nothing OS 2.6 built on top of Android 14.
### Camera
In terms of optics, the device flaunts a dual camera setup on its back. The primary sensor is a 50MP shooter accompanied by a 2MP depth sensor. Upfront, there is a 16MP snapper for selfies and video calls. As for the videos, the rear camera supports 4K res videos at 30fps. Moreover, you also get TrueLens Engine 2.) on this phone providing Ultra XDR, AI Vivid Modes, Motion Capture, and Night Mode.
### Battery and Charging
Fueling the phone is a 5000mAh battery with 33W charging support. It also supports 5W reverse wired charging. Connectivity features include 5G, WiFi 6, Bluetooth 5.3, GPS, and a USB Type-C port.

## CMF Phone 2 Pro Overview
### Design and Display
What if your phone didn’t just look different but _felt_ different too? That’s the vibe CMF is going for with the CMF Phone 2 Pro, a smartphone that offers a pleasantly personalized alternative to the typical glass slabs. Much like its predecessor, this phone comes with a user-replaceable back cover which you can unscrew and swap out in minutes. It’s a modular touch you don’t often see, especially in this price range.
The design also packs subtle durability perks. It carries an IP54 rating and can survive water splashes and even shallow dips (up to 25cm for 20 minutes), according to the manufacturer. CMF is shipping the Phone 2 Pro in four colors in Nepal: White, Black, Orange, and Light Green.
Flip it over, and you’re greeted with a massive 6.77-inch AMOLED display. It’s bright peaking at a crazy 3000 nits and supports HDR10+ and Ultra HDR, making it great for watching vivid, contrast-heavy content. With 120Hz refresh rate and 1 billion colors, this panel isn’t just smooth; it’s gorgeous.
### Performance
At the core of the Phone 2 Pro is the MediaTek Dimensity 7300 Pro chip, built on a power-efficient 4nm process. The CPU here includes four high-performance Cortex-A78 cores, and it’s paired with a Mali-G615 MC2 GPU for graphics.
This setup is backed by 8GB of RAM and up to 256GB of internal storage, with the bonus of microSD card support. The phone boots on Android 15 right out of the box, topped with Nothing OS 3.2. CMF is promising 3 major Android updates, which is reassuring in a world where midrange phones often get left behind.
### Camera
This is where the Phone 2 Pro really turns up the heat. On the back, you get a triple camera system featuring a 50MP main sensor, a 50MP telephoto lens with 2x optical zoom, and an 8MP ultrawide shooter. That’s a solid, versatile combo for a phone in this segment.
For video lovers, it supports 4K recording at 30fps, and there’s gyro-EIS for steadier shots. Up front, a 16MP selfie camera gets the job done for video calls and social media snaps with 1080p video support.
### Battery and Charging
Keeping the lights on is a 5000mAh battery, which should comfortably last a full day. It supports 33W wired charging and also comes with 5W reverse wired charging, letting you top up accessories like earbuds on the go.
Connectivity-wise, you get the usual suspects: 5G, WiFi 6, Bluetooth 5.3, and NFC (depending on the region). And yes, there’s a USB Type-C port, but no headphone jack you probably saw that coming.

# Samsung Galaxy M36: Overview
**Display and Cameras**
The Samsung Galaxy M36 sports a big 6.7-inch AMOLED screen with crisp Full HD+ resolution and a super-smooth 120Hz refresh rate great for scrolling and streaming. Protected by Gorilla Glass Victus+, the display is tough against scratches. Up front, there’s a 13MP selfie camera tucked neatly inside a waterdrop notch.
**Camera**
At the back, you get a triple-camera setup that covers all the basics. There’s a 50MP main sensor for detailed shots, an 8MP ultrawide lens for group photos or landscapes, and a 2MP macro lens for close-ups. It’s a solid everyday camera combo for casual photography lovers in Nepal.
**Performance and Software**
Powering the Galaxy M36 is Samsung’s own Exynos 1380 chip, paired with either 6GB or 8GB of RAM. Storage goes up to 256GB, giving you plenty of space for apps and photos. It runs on One UI 7 based on Android 15, and Samsung promises 6 major Android updates an excellent deal for long-term users in Nepal. The 5,000mAh battery lasts all day and supports 25W fast charging via USB-C.
**Who It’s For / Ideal Use**
The Galaxy M36 is made for people in Nepal who want a reliable mid-range phone with a great screen, long battery life, and future-proof software support. Whether you’re a student, a casual gamer, or someone who just needs a dependable phone for daily use, this one ticks all the right boxes.

## Realme 14T 5G Overview
The Realme 14T 5G features a 6.67-inch AMOLED display with a 120Hz refresh rate and up to 2100 nits peak brightness. It is powered by the MediaTek Dimensity 6300 chipset, paired with up to 12GB of RAM and 256GB of internal storage. The phone includes a dual rear camera setup with a 50MP main sensor and a 2MP secondary lens, along with a 16MP front camera. It runs on Android 15, has a 6000mAh battery with 45W fast charging support, and skips both the headphone jack and NFC.
### Performance 
Instead of going with a high-end chip, Realme chose the MediaTek Dimensity 6300, and honestly, that was a smart move for this phone’s purpose. Whether it’s social scrolling, YouTube, messaging, or light gaming, things move smoothly without overheating or draining the battery too fast. It runs Android 15 with Realme UI 6.0, and the software feels clean nothing bloated or sluggish. You get up to 12GB of RAM and 256GB of storage, which is more than enough for most people.
### Battery 
There’s a 6000mAh battery inside, and that’s where the 14T quietly shines. You can go a full day and a half, maybe even two, on a single charge if you're not constantly gaming or streaming. It supports 45W wired charging, and gets to about 50% in half an hour quick enough for most daily routines. There’s no wireless charging, but it does support bypass charging, which is useful when you're plugged in for a longer gaming session.
### Display 
The 6.67-inch AMOLED display is actually one of the highlights here. It’s bright (up to 2100 nits), smooth thanks to the 120Hz refresh rate, and has slim bezels that make it feel more immersive than you’d expect at this price. Whether you're binge-watching or just checking the news, the screen stays sharp and easy on the eyes. Colors are vibrant, but not oversaturated it strikes a nice balance.
### Camera
On the back, the Realme 14T has a 50MP main camera, paired with a very basic 2MP sensor. It’s not trying to replace a DSLR, but it does its job well for everyday shots good light, decent detail, and not much fuss. Video maxes out at 1080p@60fps, and while there's no 4K, it has gyro-EIS, which helps with shaky hands. The 16MP selfie camera is clean and simple, perfect for video calls and social posts.
### Sound & Connectivity
There are stereo speakers that are loud enough for casual media and calls, and while there’s no headphone jack, wireless audio works well via Bluetooth 5.3. It also supports 24-bit/192kHz Hi-Res audio, which audiophiles might appreciate. Connectivity-wise, it checks most boxes with 5G, Wi-Fi ac, and solid GPS coverage. No NFC here, and no FM radio either, but it’s otherwise well-equipped for daily use.

### Moto G85 5G: Overview
The Moto G85 5G is a stylish and feature-packed smartphone that builds on the popular G-series design language. It offers three attractive color options: Olive Green and Cobalt Blue with a vegan leather finish, and Urban Grey with a sleek PMMA material. The phone features a 6.67-inch FHD+ pOLED display with a smooth 120Hz refresh rate, 240Hz touch sampling, and vibrant 10-bit color depth, making it perfect for videos and gaming. With up to 1,600 nits peak brightness, it ensures excellent visibility even in bright sunlight.
Under the hood, the Moto G85 5G is powered by the new Qualcomm Snapdragon 6s Gen 3 chipset, delivering solid performance for multitasking and 5G connectivity. It comes with 8GB or 12GB of RAM and 256GB of internal storage, expandable up to 1TB with a microSD card, offering ample space for apps, photos, and videos.
The camera setup includes a 50MP primary lens with OIS for sharp, stable shots and an 8MP ultrawide lens that doubles as a macro shooter. On the front, there’s a 32MP selfie camera that also supports face recognition.
The phone is equipped with a 5,000mAh battery and supports 30W fast charging for all-day usage. Additional features include stereo speakers, dual microphones, eSIM support for dual SIM functionality, and modern connectivity options like 5G, WiFi 5, Bluetooth v5.1, and NFC. With its premium features and sleek design, the Moto G85 5G is a great choice for those looking for a versatile and stylish 5G smartphone.

## Vivo V50 Lite 4G Overview
### Display and Design
The Vivo V50 Lite has a matte-finished back, a flat-edged design, and two cameras arranged in circular modules that are vertically aligned. It features minimum bezels and a centered hole-punch display. The camera positioning, frame structure, and general look are all the same as those of the Vivo Y300.
A 6.77-inch AMOLED screen with FHD+ resolution is included with the V50 Lite 4G. It also has a 32MP front camera with a punch-hole cutout and a smooth 120Hz refresh rate. Both gold and black are color options for the gadget.
### Performance and Software
This smartphone is powered by a Qualcomm Snapdragon 685 CPU. Its octa-core CPU has two clusters of Kryo 265 cores: four power-efficient Kryo 265 Silver cores (Cortex-A53) and four high-performance Kryo 265 Gold cores (Cortex-A73 variant). Additionally, it has 256GB of internal storage and 8GB of RAM.
### Camera Setup
The V50 Lite 4G has a dual-camera setup on the back. It has a 2MP bokeh camera for portrait effects in addition to a 50MP primary camera with an IMX882 sensor.
### Battery and Durability
The device's enormous 6,500mAh battery supports 90W wired rapid charging. It has an IP65 water and dust resistance rating, indicating its durability. Additionally, it satisfies military-grade drop resistance specifications MIL-STD-810H.

# Honor X9c Smart Overview
## Design and Display
The Honor X9c Smart features a familiar yet refined design. It retains the circular camera module and hole-punch panel upfront. The slightly curved middle frame ensures a comfortable grip, making it easy to hold. The phone is built to be sturdy, with 5-star drop resistance protection and water resistance. The display is a 6.8-inch flat TFT LCD panel, offering a resolution of 2412 x 1080 and a 120Hz refresh rate. While it isn't an AMOLED display, the TFT LCD still provides a clear and smooth visual experience.
## Performance
Under the hood, the Honor X9c is powered by a Dimensity 7025 Ultra SoC. This 4nm chip includes two Cortex-A78 cores running at 2.5GHz and six Cortex-A55 cores at 2.0GHz. The IMG BXM-8-256 GPU handles graphics, ensuring smooth performance. The phone comes with 8GB of RAM and 256GB of internal storage, providing ample space for apps and media. It runs on MagicOS 9.0, built on top of Android 14, offering a seamless user experience.
## Camera
The Honor X9c Smart is equipped with a dual-camera setup. The primary camera is a 108MP sensor with an f/1.75 aperture, capable of capturing detailed and high-quality photos. The secondary camera is a 5MP Ultrawide unit, perfect for wide-angle shots. Upfront, there is a 16MP camera for selfies and video calls. While the camera setup is impressive, the Honor X9c can only record videos in 1080p resolution.
## Battery, Charging, and Connectivity
The Honor X9c Smart is powered by a 5800mAh Li-ion Polymer battery, providing long-lasting power. It supports 35W wired fast charging, allowing the battery to charge quickly. Connectivity options include 5G, WiFi 6 (Dual-band), Bluetooth 5.3, NFC, and a USB-C port. For added security, the phone features a side-mounted fingerprint scanner.

### Xiaomi Redmi Note 14 Pro 5G: Overview
#### Design and Display
The Redmi Note 14 Pro 5G features a premium design with a square camera module, a curved middle frame, and a curved display. Unlike its 4G counterpart, it boasts a proper IP68 rating, offering superior protection against dust and water.  
The display is a 6.67-inch AMOLED panel with an FHD+ resolution, a 120Hz refresh rate, and a peak brightness of 3000 nits, making it ideal for vibrant visuals. It also includes Corning Gorilla Glass Victus 2 for enhanced durability. The smartphone is available in Lavender Purple, Midnight Black, and Coral Green color options.
#### Performance
Under the hood, the Redmi Note 14 Pro 5G is powered by the Mediatek Dimensity 7300 Ultra chipset, offering robust performance and energy efficiency, thanks to its 4nm architecture. It is paired with 8GB or 12GB of LPDDR5 RAM and storage options of 256GB or 512GB UFS 2.2 for fast multitasking and storage access.  
The phone runs on Xiaomi HyperOS, built on top of Android 14, ensuring a smooth and up-to-date software experience.
#### Cameras
The camera system on the Redmi Note 14 Pro 5G is impressive, including:
  * A 200MP primary sensor with Optical Image Stabilization (OIS)
  * An 8MP ultra-wide lens
  * A 2MP macro lens


This camera setup supports advanced AI features like AI Erase Pro and AI Beautify, and it offers 4K video recording capabilities at 24/30fps, which is a step up from the 4G model. The front camera is a 20MP sensor, perfect for high-quality selfies and video calls.
#### Battery and Charging
The phone is backed by a 5110mAh battery with support for 45W fast charging, ensuring quicker recharge times and extended usage.
#### Connectivity and Other Features
The Redmi Note 14 Pro 5G supports a wide range of connectivity features, including:
  * 5G support
  * WiFi 6E
  * Bluetooth 5.4
  * NFC
  * USB Type-C port


Other standout features are:
  * An in-display fingerprint scanner for secure and convenient access
  * A Dolby-powered dual stereo speaker setup for immersive sound quality.

The Xiaomi Redmi Note 14 Pro 5G emerges as a powerful mid-range smartphone with flagship-level features like 4K video recording, 5G connectivity, and a high-end display, while maintaining a competitive price point.

## Nothing Phone (2a): A Solid Mid-Ranger
The Nothing Phone (2a) is a mid-range smartphone that retains the iconic Glyph Interface while introducing several improvements in design, performance, and camera capabilities.
#### Design and Display
The Nothing Phone (2a) features a unique transparent design with a refined Glyph Interface. The Glyph Interface now consists of three curved LED strips around the camera module, offering a more subtle yet functional aesthetic. The phone is IP54 rated for dust and water resistance, ensuring durability. It has a slightly curved back for better grip and a matte polycarbonate frame with recycled aluminum for rigidity.
The display is a 6.7-inch AMOLED panel with a 120Hz refresh rate, FHD+ resolution (1080 x 2400 pixels), and a peak brightness of 1300 nits. It offers 394 PPI density, 10-bit color support, and a screen-to-body ratio of over 90%, providing vibrant visuals and smooth interactions.
#### Performance and Memory
Under the hood, the Nothing Phone (2a) is powered by MediaTek’s Dimensity 7200 Pro SoC, an octa-core processor built on TSMC’s 2nd gen 4nm node. It features 2 Cortex A715 prime cores running at 2.8GHz and 6 Cortex A510 secondary cores at 2.0GHz. The GPU is Arm Mali-G610 MC4, supported by HyperEngine 5.0 for efficient graphical performance. The phone includes 12GB of RAM with an additional 8GB of virtual RAM and 128/256GB of UFS 3.1 storage. An advanced liquid cooling system ensures optimal thermal management. 
The device runs on Nothing OS 2.5, built on Android 14, promising three years of major OS updates and four years of security updates.
#### Camera
The Nothing Phone (2a) boasts a dual-camera setup with a 50MP main camera featuring a 1/1.15-inch sensor and OIS, coupled with a 50MP ultrawide camera with a 1/2.76-inch sensor. The main camera supports 4K video recording at 30fps. The front camera is a 32MP Sony IMX615 sensor, perfect for high-quality selfies and video calls.
#### Battery, Charging, and Connectivity
The phone is powered by a 5000mAh battery, supporting 45W fast charging. Connectivity options include 5G, Wi-Fi 6, Bluetooth 5.3, GPS, NFC, and a USB Type-C 2.0 port. The phone also features an in-display fingerprint scanner for secure biometric authentication.
Overall, the Nothing Phone (2a) offers a compelling blend of unique design, robust performance, and advanced camera capabilities, making it a standout choice in the mid-range segment.

# Honor 400 Lite: Overview
**Stylish Design and Bright AMOLED Display**
The Honor 400 Lite brings a modern design that feels both premium and practical. Its flat frame and slim body make it easy to hold, while the back design gives off an iPhone-like vibe thanks to its rectangular camera module. The phone weighs just 171 grams and measures only 7.29mm thick, making it super comfortable to use daily. It comes in two stylish color options in Nepal—Mars Green and Velvet Gray. Up front, you get a 6.7-inch AMOLED display with a 120Hz refresh rate and a resolution of 2412 x 1080 pixels. What really stands out is the peak HDR brightness of 3,500 nits, which makes the screen easy to view even under bright sunlight.The phone has an IP65 rating, so it's splash-resistant—good for everyday use but not for full underwater dives. That said, Honor says you can take photos underwater, and it can reportedly survive drops from up to 6 feet. For security, there’s an in-display fingerprint scanner, and the display is certified by TÜV Rheinland and SGS, which means less eye strain from flickering during long use.
**Decent Performance and All-Day Battery**
Performance-wise, the Honor 400 Lite is powered by the MediaTek Dimensity 7025-Ultra processor. It features Cortex A78 cores at 2.5GHz, which should be more than enough for daily use, social media, and even some gaming. On the graphics side, it uses the IMG BXM-8-256 GPU, which handles casual games well. The phone comes with 8GB or 12GB of RAM and 256GB of storage, giving you enough space for apps, videos, and photos. It runs on MagicOS 9.0, based on Android 15, though software support duration hasn’t been confirmed yet. Powering everything is a 5230mAh battery, backed by 35W fast charging, which should easily last through a full day of use.
**Sharp Cameras and Smart AI Features**
On the camera front, the Honor 400 Lite features a 108MP main sensor with 3x lossless zoom and an f/1.75 aperture, promising sharp and clear photos in daylight. It also includes a 5MP ultrawide lens that can also act as a depth sensor. A cool extra is the AI camera button below the power key, which can instantly launch the camera, take photos or videos, zoom in, and even search for objects when held down. With its mix of smart features and clean design, the Honor 400 Lite offers great value for buyers in Nepal looking for a stylish and capable mid-range smartphone.

## Vivo V50 Lite 5G Overview
### Design and Display
The Vivo V50 Lite 5G has the same design as the 4G variant, with a pill-shaped camera island, a matte back, and flat edges. It has a 6.7-inch OLED display up front with a refresh rate of 120 Hz, 1080+ resolution, and a maximum brightness of 1,800 nits. The gadget has an optical fingerprint sensor under the screen for security.
Because of its IP65 rating, the phone is resistant to dust and weak water sprays. Vivo also offers a personalized protective case that protects the screen from drops and tumbles by utilizing air-cushion technology. The Vivo V50 Lite 5G is available in Titanium Gold, Fancy Purple, Silk Green, and Phantom Black (with a purple tint).
### Performance 
An octa-core MediaTek Dimensity 6300 processor with two Cortex A76 cores and six Cortex A55 cores powers the Vivo V50 Lite 5G. It has a Mali-G57 MP2 GPU for graphics. This combination ought to do daily chores with ease and even provide respectable gaming performance. Additionally, the phone has 256GB or 512GB of UFS 2.2 storage and 8GB or 12GB of LPDDR4X RAM. There isn't a microSD slot for more storage, either. You will receive Android 15 on the software side.
### Battery
Vivo asserts that even after five years of use, the device's enormous 6,500mAh battery will maintain at least 80% of its capacity. Up to 10.5 hours of game time is possible on a full charge, which is remarkable for a gadget with such a massive battery.
### Camera and Other Features
The Vivo V50 Lite 5G has an 8MP ultra-wide camera in addition to a 50MP Sony IMX8882 primary sensor. Notably, the 4G model lacked the ultra-wide camera. In addition to the primary sensor, there is a 2MP assist camera. The phone has a 32MP front camera, the same as the 4G model, for taking selfies.
This phone has Bluetooth V5.4 capability and is anticipated to have Wi-Fi 5 (AC) built in. To improve the audio and photographic experience, the phone also features stereo speakers and a ring flash on the back. You will also receive an AI Erase 2.0 tool in addition to that.
