**Samsung Galaxy A26 5G Overview**
**Design and Display**
The Samsung Galaxy A26 5G is designed with a sleek and modern aesthetic. It features a slimmer build compared to its predecessor, the Galaxy A25 5G, measuring 164 x 77.5 x 7.7 mm and weighing 200 grams. This makes it comfortable to hold and easy to carry around. The phone is available in three stylish color options: White, Black, and Mint, catering to different preferences. The highlight of the design is its 6.7-inch AMOLED display, which offers a 120Hz refresh rate and a resolution of 2340 x 1080p. This high refresh rate ensures smooth scrolling and a more responsive user experience. Additionally, the display boasts a peak brightness of 1000 nits, making it perfect for viewing content in various lighting conditions.
**Performance and Software**
Under the hood, the Galaxy A26 5G is powered by Samsung’s Exynos 1380 chipset, which provides a balanced performance for everyday use. The device supports up to 8GB of RAM and up to 256GB of internal storage, which can be expanded via a microSD card up to 2TB. This ample storage capacity ensures that users can store a significant amount of apps, photos, and videos without worrying about running out of space. The phone runs on Android 15 with Samsung’s One UI 7, offering a clean and intuitive user interface. Samsung guarantees 6 major Android updates, ensuring that the device stays up-to-date with the latest features and security patches. While the device is capable of handling most tasks efficiently, it may not be the best choice for avid gamers who require high-performance hardware.
**Cameras**
The Galaxy A26 5G is equipped with a versatile triple-camera setup on the back, making it a great choice for photography enthusiasts. The main camera features a 50MP sensor with Optical Image Stabilization (OIS), ensuring clear and stable photos even in low-light conditions. The 8MP ultrawide sensor allows for capturing wider landscapes and group photos, while the 2MP macro sensor is perfect for close-up shots of small objects. On the front, the phone boasts a 13MP selfie camera, which is ideal for taking high-quality selfies and making video calls. The combination of these cameras provides users with a comprehensive photography experience, covering various shooting scenarios.
**Battery and Additional Features**
The Galaxy A26 5G is powered by a substantial 5,000mAh battery, which is expected to provide all-day usage on a single charge. It supports 25W wired charging, allowing the battery to recharge quickly when needed. The device also includes a side-mounted fingerprint sensor for convenient and secure unlocking. Additionally, it offers IP67 water and dust resistance, making it more durable and suitable for use in various environments. Samsung Knox security ensures that users’ data is protected with advanced security features. The phone also features “Awesome Intelligence” capabilities, which were introduced in the latest A-series lineup, enhancing the overall user experience.
Overall, the Samsung Galaxy A26 5G is a well-rounded device that offers a good balance of design, performance, camera capabilities, and additional features. It is suitable for users who are looking for a reliable smartphone with a large display, decent performance, and excellent camera quality, all at an affordable price.

# Infinix GT 30 Pro Overview
**Performance**
The GT 30 Pro leans on MediaTek’s Dimensity 8350 Ultimate, a 4 nm chip that breezes through PUBG, Insta scrolling, and Lightroom tweaks without dropping frames. Paired with 8 GB RAM (expandable to 12 GB via memory fusion) and fast UFS 4.0 storage, apps pop open in a blink. XOS 15 on Android 15 feels lighter than past Infinix skins, and the dual-shoulder GT triggers give you console-style taps with almost zero input lag and handy for clutch matches on Nepali servers.
**Design and Display**
At first glance the 6.78-inch LTPS AMOLED steals the show: 144 Hz refresh keeps animations liquid-smooth, while 2000-nit peak brightness stays legible even under Pokhara’s midday sun. Gorilla Glass 7i fronts the panel, and a neat RGB strip on the back adds gamer flair without looking kitsch. You can pick from Blade White, Shadow Ash, or Dark Flare finishes; all three hide fingerprints better than you’d think. The squared-off frame sits comfortably in one hand, and IP64 sealing shrugs off dust on Himalayan trails.
**Camera**
A 108 MP main shooter snaps crisp daylight photos with plenty of detail for Instagram Reels, while the 8 MP ultrawide widens the scene for group shots at Pashupatinath or sunset landscapes in Sarangkot. Selfie duties fall to a 13 MP front cam that handles skin tones well and supports 4K video. Night mode is decent, pulling in enough light without turning everything into a watercolor painting.
**Battery, Charging & Extras**
The 5550 mAh cell (5200 mAh in some markets) easily powers a full day of heavy use think 7-plus hours of screen-on time. When you’re low, 45 W wired or 30 W wireless top-ups get you back to 50 % in roughly half an hour, and bypass charging keeps temps down during marathon gaming. Infinix even bundles a MagCharge Cooler that clips on magnetically and drops temps by about 30 %. Toss in stereo speakers, an in-display fingerprint reader, and 0 % EMI deals at hukut store, and you get a feature-packed mid-ranger.
**Who It’s For / Ideal Use**
If you’re looking for the “best gaming phone under 50,000 in Nepal” that can double as a daily driver, the Infinix GT 30 Pro nails the brief. It suits students who live on Mobile Legends, creators who need a bright panel for color-accurate edits, and road warriors who hate hunting for chargers. In short, anyone wanting flagship-style extras on a mid-tier budget should keep this handset on their radar.

## Honor X9c Overview
The Honor X9c is a stylish and feature-packed mid-range smartphone designed for users who prioritize durability, display quality, and battery life. With an elegant 6.78-inch AMOLED display boasting 1 billion colors, a 120Hz refresh rate, and a peak brightness of 4000 nits, the X9c delivers an immersive viewing experience with vibrant colors and smooth scrolling.
### Sleek Yet Durable Build
The device sports a premium design with dimensions of 162.8 x 75.5 x 8 mm and a lightweight build of 189g, making it comfortable to hold. Available in Titanium Purple, Titanium Black, and Jade Cyan, it exudes a sophisticated look. Despite its sleekness, the Honor X9c is IP65-rated for dust and water resistance and can withstand drops of up to 2 meters, ensuring enhanced durability.
### Powerful Performance & Storage Options
Under the hood, the Honor X9c runs on Android 14 with Magic OS 8 and is powered by the Qualcomm Snapdragon 6 Gen 1 (4nm) chipset, an efficient processor that handles everyday tasks with ease. The octa-core CPU (4x2.2 GHz Cortex-A78 & 4x1.8 GHz Cortex-A55) and Adreno 710 GPU provide a balanced mix of performance and power efficiency. The phone is available in 256GB 8GB RAM, 256GB 12GB RAM, and 512GB 12GB RAM variants, though it lacks expandable storage.
### Impressive Camera System
The Honor X9c features a triple-camera setup on the back, led by a 108MP primary sensor with PDAF and OIS for high-resolution, stabilized shots. Accompanying it is a 5MP ultrawide camera for capturing expansive landscapes. The rear camera supports 4K video recording at 30fps. On the front, a 16MP selfie camera ensures sharp and detailed self-portraits while supporting 1080p video recording.
### Long-Lasting Battery with Fast Charging
Equipped with a massive 6600mAh Silicon-Carbon Li-Ion battery, the Honor X9c is built for extended usage without frequent recharges. The 66W fast wired charging ensures quick top-ups, while reverse wired charging adds extra versatility.
### Additional Features & Connectivity
The phone features stereo speakers for an enhanced audio experience but lacks a 3.5mm headphone jack. For connectivity, it supports Wi-Fi 802.11 a/b/g/n/ac, Bluetooth 5.1, NFC, an infrared port, and USB Type-C 2.0 with OTG support. The in-display optical fingerprint sensor ensures secure and convenient unlocking.
### Network & 5G Support
The Honor X9c is 5G-ready, supporting a wide range of 2G, 3G, 4G, and 5G bands, ensuring strong connectivity across different networks.

## Xiaomi Redmi Note 14 Pro+ 5G: Overview
### Design and Display
The Redmi Note 14 Pro+ 5G takes the premium design of the Pro series to the next level. It features a square camera module, a curved middle frame, and a curved AMOLED display for an immersive viewing experience. It comes with a top-tier IP68 rating, ensuring water and dust resistance.  
The display is a 6.67-inch AMOLED panel with an FHD+ resolution, 120Hz refresh rate, and a peak brightness of 3000 nits. Additionally, it features Corning Gorilla Glass Victus 2 for enhanced durability. The device is available in Frost Blue, Midnight Black, and Lavender Purple colorways.
### Performance
At its core, the Redmi Note 14 Pro+ 5G is powered by the Qualcomm SM7635 Snapdragon 7s Gen 3 chipset, built on a 4nm process. This flagship-grade processor offers blazing-fast performance, catering to demanding tasks and gaming. It is paired with 12GB or 8GB of LPDDR5X RAM and storage options of 256GB or 512GB UFS 2.2, delivering seamless multitasking and ultra-fast data access.  
The device runs Xiaomi HyperOS, based on Android 14, for a smooth and optimized user experience.
### Cameras
The Redmi Note 14 Pro+ 5G shines in the camera department with a high-end triple-lens setup:
  * A 200MP primary sensor with OIS (Optical Image Stabilization)
  * A 18MP ultra-wide lens for expansive shots
  * A 2MP telemacro lens for detailed close-ups


The camera system supports 4K video recording at 24/30fps and 1080p video recording at 30/60/120fps, along with advanced AI features like AI Erase Pro and AI Beautify for enhanced photography. The 20MP front camera ensures stunning selfies and high-quality video calls.
### Battery and Charging
The phone is equipped with a 5110mAh battery, complemented by 120W HyperCharge technology, allowing for ultra-fast charging.
### Connectivity and Other Features
The Redmi Note 14 Pro+ 5G is packed with advanced connectivity options, including:
  * 5G with advanced network aggregation
  * WiFi 7

## Realme 14 5G: Overview
The Realme 14 5G features a 6.67-inch AMOLED display with a 120Hz refresh rate and peak brightness of 2000 nits. It is powered by the Snapdragon 6 Gen 4 processor paired with up to 12GB of RAM and 512GB of internal storage. The phone includes a 50MP main camera with OIS and a 16MP front-facing camera, both capable of recording in 1080p or higher. It runs on Android 15 with Realme UI 6.0 and houses a 6000mAh battery that supports 45W wired charging.
### Performance 
Under the hood, the Realme 14 packs Qualcomm’s new Snapdragon 6 Gen 4 chip, and for a midrange phone, it’s smooth like, genuinely smooth. App switching, gaming, even light video editing doesn’t feel sluggish. And the Adreno 810 GPU? It holds its own surprisingly well in graphics-heavy tasks. Android 15 with Realme UI 6.0 is clean, responsive, and doesn’t feel bloated.
Whether you pick the 8GB or 12GB RAM model, paired with up to 512GB of internal storage, there’s zero compromise in day-to-day use. No microSD card, but honestly, you’re unlikely to run out of room.
### Battery 
Here’s the part that stands out: 6000mAh battery. This thing is a tank. Two full days on moderate use isn’t a stretch. And when you do need to juice up, 45W fast charging brings it back to life quickly 50% in just 30 minutes. Plus, there’s bypass charging for when you're gaming and want to avoid battery heat. Smart stuff.
### Display 
The 6.67-inch AMOLED display is crisp, fluid, and bright enough to fight off direct sunlight, peaking at 2000 nits. Scrolling and gaming benefit from the 120Hz refresh rate, which makes the whole experience feel more premium than the price suggests.
### Camera
Realme didn’t overcomplicate things here. You get a single 50MP main camera with OIS and PDAF, and it shoots sharp photos that are surprisingly stable—even in low light. Video goes up to 4K@30fps, with electronic stabilization keeping things steady. The 16MP front cam handles selfies just fine, with some pleasant HDR tuning that doesn’t go overboard.
### Audio & Connectivity
Stereo speakers? Check. No headphone jack, sadly, but wireless audio works well with Bluetooth 5.2. The phone supports Wi-Fi 6, so no issues with fast networks. GPS performance is reliable thanks to multiple satellite systems onboard. NFC is missing, which might be a dealbreaker for contactless payment fans.
### Design & Build
At 196g, the Realme 14 feels substantial but not heavy. The 8mm slim profile makes it easy to hold, and while the design isn’t revolutionary, the Silver, Titanium, and Pink options give it some personality. Realme kept it clean no huge logos or odd camera bumps.

## Samsung Galaxy A54 Overview:
### Design
If you remember, Galaxy A53 shares the same design as the A52 from 2021. But Samsung has made some design changes with the A54, drawing cues from the flagship S23 series. As a result, the smartphone looks quite identical to the vanilla S23, both from the front and the back with a glass back.
It is available in three shades: Awesome Violet, Awesome Lime, and Awesome Graphite. The smartphone also bags an IP67 certification for protection against dust and water.
Moreover, the Galaxy A54 features a 6.4″ screen with a centered punch hole. It’s a Super AMOLED display with Full HD+ resolution, protected by Gorilla Glass 5. And you get 120Hz of refresh rate while the peak brightness is rated at 1000 nits.
### Camera
Moving on to the cameras, while the older A52 and A53 both had a 64MP primary lens, Samsung is changing things up for the Galaxy A54 which now sports a 50MP primary camera with OIS. It is followed by 12MP ultrawide and 5MP macro units. It has a 32MP selfie snapper on the front. Samsung has also provided Nightography for low-light imageries.
### Performance
Under the hood, the device packs the newly-announced Exynos 1380 5G processor. Based on the 5nm process, this SoC has four Cortex-A78 (@2.4 GHz) and four Cortex-A55 (@2.0 GHz) cores. Similarly, the Mali G68 MP5 GPU is there for the graphics.
Looking at the core architecture, the Exynos 1380 should deliver the same performance as the Snapdragon 778G chipset. As for the software, it boots on the latest One UI 5.1 based on Android 13. The company has pledged to provide 4 years of major OS updates with 5 years of security patch updates on the Galaxy A54.
### Rest of the specs
Furthermore, a 5000mAh battery powers the phone, whereas the charging speed is still capped at 25W. The connectivity options include 5G, WiFi 5, NFC, GPS, Bluetooth 5.3, and USB Type-C port. Likewise, you also get Dolby Atmos-tuned stereo speakers, Voice Focus, Privacy Dashboard, Samsung Knox, Samsung wallet, etc.

## Nothing Phone (2a) Plus Overview
### Display and Design
The Nothing Phone (2a) Plus features a 6.7-inch OLED display with a 1080p resolution and a 120 Hz refresh rate. Gorilla Glass 5 protects the display and the screen supports a peak brightness of 1300 nits.. The design is distinctive, with a unique owl-like appearance on the rear, similar to its predecessor. The back showcases the same glyph pattern that has become a signature of the brand. Additionally, the color has also been updated to a sleek, metallic grey-looking design.
### Performance 
Under the hood, the Nothing Phone (2a) Plus is powered by the MediaTek Dimensity 7350 processor. It includes 12GB of LPDDR5 RAM, with an additional 8GB RAM boost, and utilizes UFS 3.1 storage for efficient performance. The phone runs on Nothing OS 2.5. Special features include the TrueLens Engine, Ultra XDR, and Motion Capture.
### Camera 
The device features a dual-camera setup on the rear. The primary camera is 50MP with Optical Image Stabilization (OIS), and it is accompanied by an upgraded 50MP ultra-wide camera. The front camera is also 50MP, designed for high-resolution selfies. The phone supports 4K video recording on the rear camera and 1080p video recording on the front. Additionally, it offers 1080p slow-motion video recording.
### Battery and Charging 
The Nothing Phone (2a) Plus is equipped with a 5000 mAh battery. It supports 45W fast charging.

# **Samsung Galaxy A36 Overview**
**Design and Display**  
The Samsung Galaxy A36 is a sleek and modern smartphone that stands out with its slim and lightweight design. Measuring 6.7 inches, it features an FHD+ AMOLED display that delivers stunning visuals with a 120Hz refresh rate and a peak brightness of 1,200 nits. This combination ensures smooth scrolling and vibrant colors, making it perfect for streaming videos, gaming, and browsing the web. Available in four stylish colors—Lime, Lavender, Black, and White—the Galaxy A36 is designed with an IP67 rating for dust and water resistance, making it durable and suitable for various environments. Whether you're at the beach or in the rain, the Galaxy A36 can handle it with ease.
**Performance and Software**  
Under the hood, the Galaxy A36 is powered by the Qualcomm Snapdragon 6 Gen 3 processor, a latest-generation 4nm chip that offers reliable performance and efficiency. The phone comes with up to 8GB of RAM and up to 256GB of non-expandable storage, providing ample space for your apps, photos, and videos. To keep things cool, the Galaxy A36 features a 15% larger vapor chamber, ensuring optimal performance even during extended use. Running on Android 15 with One UI 7, the device offers a clean and intuitive interface with various AI-driven features. These include Object Recognition, Circle to Search, Auto Trim, and Best Face, enhancing your overall user experience. Samsung has also committed to providing updates for the next six years, ensuring your device stays up-to-date with the latest features and security enhancements.
**Cameras**  
The Galaxy A36 excels in photography with its versatile rear camera setup, which includes a 50MP main sensor, an 8MP wide-angle lens, and a 5MP macro sensor. This combination allows you to capture high-quality photos in various scenarios, from detailed close-ups to wide-angle landscapes. The front camera is a 12MP unit that supports HDR video, making it perfect for capturing high-quality selfies and videos. Whether you're vlogging or simply sharing moments with friends, the Galaxy A36 ensures your content looks its best. Additionally, the phone is equipped with a 5,000mAh battery that supports 45W fast charging, providing long-lasting power and quick recharging capabilities. The device also retains the under-display optical fingerprint sensor from its predecessor, the A35, ensuring secure and convenient access to your phone.
**Conclusion**  
The Samsung Galaxy A36 is a well-rounded smartphone that offers a perfect blend of design, performance, and features. With its sleek and durable design, high-quality display, powerful processor, and versatile camera setup, the Galaxy A36 is an excellent choice for those looking for a reliable and feature-rich device. Whether you're a content creator, a busy professional, or simply someone who wants a great smartphone, the Galaxy A36 has you covered.

## Nothing Phone (3a) Overview
### Body Design and Build
The Nothing Phone (3a) boasts a sleek and modern design with dimensions of 163.5 x 77.5 x 8.4 mm and a weight of 201 grams, making it compact and comfortable to hold. It supports dual Nano-SIM cards and an eSIM, offering flexible connectivity options. The phone is IP64 rated, providing protection against dust and water splashes, making it suitable for everyday use. Additionally, the back features three LED light strips with 26 addressable zones, which can be customized for notifications and camera fill light, adding a unique touch to its design.
### Display and Visuals
The Nothing Phone (3a) features a 6.77-inch AMOLED display with a resolution of 1080 x 2412 pixels and a 20:9 aspect ratio. It supports 1B colors, a 120Hz refresh rate, HDR10+, and peaks at 3000 nits, ensuring vibrant and smooth visuals. The screen is protected by Panda Glass and includes an Always On Display for convenient access to information.
### Performance and Hardware
Under the hood, the Nothing Phone (3a) runs on Android 15 with Nothing OS 3.1, powered by the Qualcomm SM7635 Snapdragon 7s Gen 3 chipset. It features an octa-core CPU and an Adreno 710 GPU, providing solid performance for everyday tasks and gaming. The phone comes with internal storage options of 256GB paired with either 8GB or 12GB of RAM, though it lacks a card slot for expandable storage.
### Camera and Imaging
The camera setup includes a triple-lens main camera with a 50 MP wide sensor featuring PDAF and OIS, a 50 MP telephoto lens with 2x optical zoom, and an 8 MP ultrawide lens. These cameras support various features like LED flash, panorama, and HDR, and can record 4K video at 30fps and 1080p video at 60/120fps with gyro-EIS. The selfie camera is a 32 MP wide sensor with HDR support and can record 1080p video at 60fps.
### Audio and Connectivity
The Nothing Phone (3a) features stereo speakers for immersive audio and supports Wi-Fi 802.11 a/b/g/n/ac/6, Bluetooth 5.4, and various positioning systems including GPS, GALILEO, GLONASS, BDS, and QZSS. It also includes NFC and USB Type-C 2.0 connectivity.
### Battery and Power
The phone is equipped with a substantial 5000 mAh battery, supporting 50W wired charging, which can reach 50% in just 19 minutes and full charge in 56 minutes.
### Colors and Availability
The Nothing Phone (3a) is available in black and other colors, offering a stylish and functional device that caters to modern users' needs.

# Honor 400: Overview
**Sleek Design and Smooth Display**
The Honor 400 carries a clean and stylish design that closely matches its Pro version. It comes in three attractive color options in Nepal with Desert Gold, Tidal Blue, and Midnight Black. The camera module is the same as the Pro, but the phone has a flat middle frame instead of a curved one. For protection, it features an IP66 rating, so it’s resistant to dust and water splashes, great for everyday use in unpredictable weather. The front side is dominated by a 6.55-inch AMOLED curved screen, which offers a sharp resolution of 2736 x 1264 pixels. The display supports 120Hz refresh rate, HDR10, and 3840Hz PWM dimming, making it smooth for scrolling and safe for the eyes. There's also a punch-hole cutout instead of a pill-shaped notch, giving it a cleaner look.
**Good Performance with Long-Term Support**
At its core, the Honor 400 is powered by the Snapdragon 7 Gen 3 processor. It’s a 4nm chip that performs well for regular tasks, social media use, and light gaming. Backed by 12GB LPDDR5X RAM and 512GB UFS 4.0 storage, this phone ensures quick app launches and plenty of room for photos, videos, and apps. It runs on Android 15, layered with MagicOS 9.0, offering a clean user experience with smart AI features like language translation and writing suggestions. What’s more, Honor guarantees 6 years of software and security updates, which is a big plus for buyers in Nepal who want reliable long-term usage without needing to upgrade often.
**Camera and Battery to Match Your Lifestyle**
The camera setup is one of the main highlights of the Honor 400. You get a 200MP main camera with OIS, perfect for detailed shots, and a 12MP ultrawide sensor that can also take close-up macro photos. While it doesn’t include a telephoto lens, the front has a solid 50MP selfie camera for clear video calls and selfies. Fueling all this is a 6000mAh silicon-carbon battery, which easily lasts more than a day. Charging is fast too, with support for 80W wired and wireless SuperCharge. Other features include WiFi 6, Bluetooth 5.4, eSIM, USB-C, and an in-display fingerprint scanner, making the Honor 400 a balanced mid-range option for users in Nepal.

# vivo V50: Overview
## Design and Display
The vivo V50 is a sleek and stylish smartphone that combines modern aesthetics with advanced technology. It features a curved AMOLED display that measures 6.77 inches, offering a stunning visual experience with a 120Hz refresh rate. This high refresh rate ensures smooth scrolling and fluid animations, making every interaction with the device a pleasure. The display supports HDR content and boasts impressive brightness levels, reaching up to 1500 nits at peak and 1300 nits under sunlight (HBM mode). The device is available in three elegant color options: Rose Red, Starry Night, and Titanium Grey. Despite its large battery, the vivo V50 maintains a slim design, making it comfortable to hold and use. It also includes an optical fingerprint scanner for secure and convenient unlocking, as well as stereo speakers for immersive audio.
## Performance and Software
Powered by the Snapdragon 7 Gen 3 chipset, the vivo V50 delivers reliable performance that can handle most games and applications at a satisfactory level. The processor is paired with up to 12GB of RAM and 512GB of storage, ensuring smooth multitasking and ample space for your media and files. While some may argue that the chipset is the same as its predecessor, the vivo V50 still offers a solid performance experience. The phone runs on Funtouch OS 15, which is based on Android 15. vivo has committed to providing three years of Android updates and four years of security patches, ensuring that your device stays up-to-date and secure over time.
## Cameras
One of the standout features of the vivo V50 is its Zeiss-branded triple-camera setup. The rear camera system includes a 50MP primary sensor with OIS (Optical Image Stabilization) and a 50MP ultrawide lens, allowing you to capture stunning photos with exceptional detail and clarity. The front camera is equally impressive, featuring a 50MP sensor that ensures high-quality selfies and video calls. The device supports Zeiss Multi-Focal Portraits, including the popular Biotar Portrait Mode and 35mm B-Speed Mode, which add a professional touch to your photos. The Smart Aura Light enhances lighting conditions, making it easier to take great shots in various environments. Both the front and rear cameras offer HDR support and 4K video recording, ensuring that you can capture high-quality content no matter the situation.
## Battery and Charging
The vivo V50 is equipped with a powerful 6,000mAh battery, providing long-lasting power to keep you connected throughout the day. This is an upgrade from its predecessor’s 5500mAh battery, ensuring even better battery life. The device supports 90W wired charging, which means you can quickly recharge your phone and get back to using it in no time. Additionally, the vivo V50 supports Wi-Fi 6 + 6GHz band, offering faster and more stable wireless connectivity. Whether you’re streaming videos, playing games, or simply browsing the web, the vivo V50’s battery and charging capabilities ensure that you can do so without worrying about running out of power.
## Conclusion
The vivo V50 is a well-rounded smartphone that offers a combination of stylish design, powerful performance, impressive cameras, and long-lasting battery life. With its curved AMOLED display, Snapdragon 7 Gen 3 chipset, Zeiss-branded cameras, and 6,000mAh battery with 90W charging, the vivo V50 is a great choice for anyone looking for a reliable and feature-packed device. Whether you’re a photography enthusiast, a gamer, or simply someone who wants a high-quality smartphone, the vivo V50 is definitely worth considering.

## OnePlus Nord 4 Overview
### Display and Design
The OnePlus Nord 4 features a 6.74-inch Tianma U8+ OLED display with a resolution of 2772×1240 pixels and a 120Hz refresh rate. The display has a peak brightness of 2150 nits. On the design side, the Nord 4 comes with a refreshing look.
The OnePlus Nord 4 features a straightforward design, which they call the “only metal unibody smartphone on the planet in the 5G era” in a dual-tone rear panel. The smartphone comes in three colorways; the Mercurial Silver features two large camera lenses and a flash in the upper section, while the lower section has a textured finish with diagonal lines. At the same time, other colors remain Obsidian Midnight and Oasis Green.
### Performance and Storage
The Nord 4 is powered by the Snapdragon 7+ Gen3 processor, an upgrade from the Nord 3’s Dimensity 9000. Talking of this processor, it is an Octa-core silicon with one prime Cortex-X4 core at 2.8GHz, four Cortex-A720 cores at 2.6GHz, and three Cortex-A520 cores at 1.9GHz. To compare, this chipset provides flagship-level performance, having comparable benchmark scores with the last-gen Titan Snapdragon 8 Gen 2 and even closer to this year’s 8s Gen 3 processor.
It includes up to 12GB LPDDR5X RAM and up to 256GB UFS 4.0 storage. Moreover, the OnePlus Nord 4 also features 0.0179 square meters of cooling technology. The smartphone runs on Android 14. OnePlus promises four major Android updates and six years of security updates.
### Camera
The rear camera setup includes a 50MP main camera (LYT600) with OIS and an 8MP ultra-wide camera. The front camera is 16MP. Moreover, the OnePlus Nord 4 has an in-display fingerprint sensor and stereo speakers with Dolby Atmos support. The device has a 5500mAh battery and supports 100W SuperVOOC fast charging. The Nord 4 includes an IR Blaster, 0809 AAC linear motor, an alert slider as well

## OnePlus 13R: A Semi-Flagship Powerhouse for Nepal
### Design and Display
The OnePlus 13R boasts a sleek and modern design with a flat frame and a circular camera module, reminiscent of the iconic OnePlus style. It features a premium metal frame with an IP65 rating, ensuring protection against dust and water splashes. Available in Nebula Noir and Astral Trail colors, this device combines aesthetics with durability. The display is a standout feature, offering a 6.78-inch ProXDR OLED panel with a 1.5K resolution and LTPO 4.1 technology, allowing dynamic refresh rates from 1Hz to 120Hz. This screen not only enhances visual quality but also optimizes battery life. It also secures 5 stars SGS Screen Reliability certification, TUV Rheinland Intelligent Eye Care, TUV Rheinland Intelligent Eye Care 4.0 Dolby Vision, HDR 10+, and HDR Vivid standards.
### Performance
Under the hood, the OnePlus 13R is powered by the Snapdragon 8 Gen 3 SoC, a last-gen flagship chip that still delivers exceptional performance. It features a 4nm architecture with a prime Cortex-X4 core at 3.3GHz, three Cortex-A720 cores at 3.2GHz, two Cortex-A720 at 3.0GHz, and two Cortex-A520 cores at 2.3GHz. The Adreno 750 GPU ensures smooth graphics performance. OnePlus has paired this chip with 12GB or 16GB of RAM and 256GB or 512GB of UFS 4.0 storage, providing ample space for apps and media. The device runs on OxygenOS 15, built on top of Android 15, offering a seamless and intuitive user experience.
### Camera
The OnePlus 13R’s camera setup is designed to capture stunning photos and videos. It features a triple rear camera system, headlined by a 50MP Sony LYT-700 primary sensor with a 1/1.56-inch size and OIS for sharp and stable shots. Complementing this is a 50MP telephoto lens with 2X optical zoom and an 8MP ultra-wide-angle camera for capturing expansive landscapes. The front camera is a 16MP sensor, perfect for high-quality selfies and clear video calls. This versatile camera system performs exceptionally well across various lighting conditions and scenarios.
### Battery, Charging, and Connectivity
Equipped with a substantial 6000mAh battery, the OnePlus 13R ensures long-lasting usage, making it ideal for users who need a reliable device throughout the day. It supports 80W SuperVOOC fast charging, allowing the battery to charge quickly. The OnePlus 13R also offers robust connectivity options, including 5G, WiFi 7, Bluetooth 5.4, GPS, NFC, and a USB 2.0 Type-C port. For added security, it features an in-display fingerprint reader.
### Pricing
The OnePlus 13R is competitively priced, offering flagship-level features at a more accessible price point. In Nepal, this device is expected to be a popular choice for those seeking a balance between performance, design, and affordability.
The OnePlus 13R is a compelling choice for users in Nepal who want a powerful, stylish, and reliable smartphone without breaking the bank. With its impressive display, robust performance, versatile camera, and long-lasting battery, it ticks all the right boxes.

# Honor 400 Pro: Overview
**Premium Look, Built to Last**
The Honor 400 Pro doesn’t just perform well—it looks the part too. Its slim profile, just 8.1mm thick, paired with a weight of 205 grams, gives it a nice balance between solid and sleek. In Nepal, it's available in two classy finishes: Midnight Black and Lunar Grey. The phone comes with IP68 and IP69 ratings, meaning it's protected against both dust and strong water pressure. Whether you’re caught in the rain or out on a hike, it can handle the elements. Up front, it sports a 6.7-inch AMOLED display that’s sharp, colorful, and fluid thanks to its 1224 x 2700 resolution and 120Hz refresh rate. With a peak brightness of 5000 nits, visibility outdoors is never an issue.
**Fast, Fluid, and Future-Ready**
Performance is a real highlight on the Honor 400 Pro. It runs on the Snapdragon 8 Gen 3 chip, built with 4nm technology—one of the most powerful mobile processors right now. Whether you're switching between apps, editing videos, or playing high-end games, this phone doesn’t flinch. You also get 12GB of RAM and up to 512GB of internal storage, giving you plenty of space and speed. Out of the box, it runs on MagicOS 9, which is layered over Android 15. For users in Nepal, one of the biggest perks is Honor’s 6-year update guarantee, which is rare and adds great long-term value.
**Cameras Packed with Power and AI**
Photography is another area where the Honor 400 Pro shines. The rear setup includes a 200MP main sensor with OIS for clearer shots, a 50MP telephoto lens with 3x optical zoom, and a 12MP ultrawide lens for capturing more in every frame. On the front, there’s a 50MP selfie camera alongside a 2MP depth sensor, both housed in a pill-shaped notch. But this phone isn’t just about megapixels. It also brings helpful AI tools like deepfake detection, live call translation, and writing assistance. Backed by a 6000mAh battery that supports 100W fast charging and 50W wireless charging, the phone keeps up with your day. It also includes Wi-Fi 7, Bluetooth 5.4, NFC, and an in-display fingerprint scanner. For anyone in Nepal looking for a high-end Android experience that ticks every box, the Honor 400 Pro is an easy recommendation.

## Apple iPhone 14: A Solid Upgrade
The iPhone 14 is a reliable mid-range smartphone that retains the iconic design of its predecessor while introducing notable improvements in performance, camera capabilities, and safety features.
#### Design and Display
The iPhone 14 features the same design as its predecessor, with a large notch on the front and diagonally aligned camera lenses on the back. The entire body is made of aerospace-grade aluminum, offering durability and a premium feel. It is dust and water-resistant to IP68 standards, ensuring protection against everyday hazards. The front is protected by a Ceramic Shield, providing enhanced scratch resistance. The 6.1-inch SuperRetina XDR OLED display supports Dolby Vision HDR, P3, and True Tone, with a peak HDR brightness of 1200 nits and a refresh rate of 60Hz. While it lacks ProMotion, the display still offers vibrant visuals and excellent clarity.
#### Performance
Under the hood, the iPhone 14 is powered by the A15 Bionic chip, a 5-core GPU version of the SoC found in last year’s iPhone 13 Pro models. This chip provides a performance boost of 18% compared to its predecessor. The iPhone 14 is available in three storage options: 128GB, 256GB, and 512GB, catering to various user needs.
#### Cameras
The iPhone 14 features a dual-camera setup on the back, including a 12MP wide-angle primary sensor with a larger f/1.5 aperture and sensor-shift OIS, paired with a 12MP ultra-wide-angle lens. These cameras, combined with the new Photonic Engine, deliver significant improvements in low-light performance. The Photonic Engine enhances the main sensor’s mid-to-low-light performance by 2.5x and the ultrawide and selfie camera’s performance by 2x. For the first time, the front camera also features autofocus, making selfies and video chats sharper and clearer.
#### Battery
The iPhone 14 offers impressive battery life, providing up to 80 hours of audio playback and up to 20 hours of video playback. It charges with a 20W adapter, reaching 50% capacity in about 30 minutes. The phone also supports 15W MagSafe Wireless and 7.5W Qi wireless charging, offering flexible charging options.
#### Extras
The iPhone 14 series introduces several safety features. The “Crash Detection” feature uses the phone’s high-dynamic range gyroscope and dual-core accelerometer to automatically connect to emergency services in the event of an accident. Additionally, the Emergency SOS via Satellite feature allows users to send messages even without cellular connection by pointing the phone at a satellite. Apple’s specialized software guides users to the optimal satellite position, ensuring reliable communication in emergencies.
Overall, the iPhone 14 is a well-rounded device that balances familiar design with enhanced performance, camera capabilities, and innovative safety features, making it a solid choice for Apple enthusiasts.

## Samsung Galaxy Z Flip 6: A Refined Foldable
#### Design
The Samsung Galaxy Z Flip 6 continues to refine the iconic clamshell form factor, offering a slimmer profile at just 14.9mm thickness when folded. The device is more durable, thanks to its armor aluminum frame and an IP48 rating for dust and water resistance. The camera cutouts on the front panel now match the frame color, adding to the aesthetic appeal.
#### Display
The Z Flip 6 features a 3.4-inch cover display with a 60Hz refresh rate and a resolution of 720x728 pixels. The main display is a 6.7-inch Dynamic AMOLED 2X panel with FHD+ resolution and a 120Hz refresh rate, protected by Corning Gorilla Glass Victus 2. This setup ensures vibrant visuals and smooth interactions.
#### Camera
The camera setup on the Z Flip 6 includes a 50MP primary sensor with OIS and a 12MP ultrawide camera. The primary camera also offers 2x in-sensor zoom and up to 10x digital zoom. The front camera is a 10MP snapper, perfect for selfies and video calls. Both rear and front cameras support 4K 60fps video recording.
#### Processor and AI Features
The Z Flip 6 is powered by the Snapdragon 8 Gen 3 SoC for Galaxy, ensuring top-tier performance. It comes with 12GB of RAM and 256GB of UFS 4.0 storage. The device also features VC cooling for better heat management. Galaxy AI features like Circle to Search, Generative Edit, and Chat Assist enhance productivity and convenience.
#### Battery and Others
The Z Flip 6 includes a 4000mAh battery, offering improved battery life. It supports 25W fast charging, 10W wireless charging, and 4.5W reverse wireless charging. Connectivity options include 5G, VoNR, WiFi 6, Bluetooth 5.3, GPS, NFC, and a USB 3.2 Gen 1 Type-C port.
The Samsung Galaxy Z Flip 6 is a refined and powerful foldable smartphone, offering a sleek design, high-quality displays, impressive camera capabilities, and robust performance.

With the OnePlus 12, you can connect, create, and explore the world in ways that are truly remarkable. It's more than just a phone.

The OnePlus 12, which combines style and utility with a sleek and ergonomic design, is a work of art. A comfortable grip and a sumptuous feel are guaranteed by the high-quality materials and painstaking attention to detail. The device's breathtaking AMOLED display will engross you in your favorite entertainment with its rich blacks, vivid colors, and superb clarity.
## Cameras
The cutting-edge camera system on the OnePlus 12 produces amazing images and videos under any lighting circumstance. The state-of-the-art Snapdragon 8 Gen 3 processor, a technological marvel that offers remarkable speed and performance, powers the OnePlus 12. The Snapdragon 8 Gen 3 processor in the OnePlus 12 will never let you down, whether you're gaming, multitasking, or using resource-intensive apps.

### OnePlus 13 Overview: A Leap in Design, Performance, and Features
The OnePlus 13 introduces a refined design, moving away from the bold camera module of its predecessor to a simpler, less protruding island. This minimalist approach gives the device a clean, modern look. A significant upgrade is the inclusion of IP68 and IP69 dust and water resistance, a leap from the OnePlus 12's IP65 rating. The screen features a flatter panel with slightly curved edges, providing a more stable viewing experience. The display is BOE's X2 OLED with 8T LTPO technology, offering QHD resolution and a peak brightness of up to 4500 nits. The 6.82-inch display is slightly shorter but wider, and it now includes a more secure ultrasonic fingerprint sensor under the screen, enhancing security and convenience.
### Powerful Performance and Gaming Enhancements
Under the hood, the OnePlus 13 is powered by the Snapdragon 8 Elite, fabricated on TSMC’s 3nm process. This processor delivers a 45% boost in CPU performance and a 44% improvement in efficiency, thanks to new Oryon prime and performance cores. The Adreno 830 GPU provides up to 40% better performance, making the OnePlus 13 a formidable gaming device. To enhance the gaming experience, the phone includes a new, larger gaming vibration motor, which is touted as the biggest in any Android phone. Memory configurations start at 12GB of LPDDR5x RAM and 256GB of UFS 4.0 storage, with options up to 24GB RAM and 1TB storage. The OnePlus 13 runs on ColorOS 15 in China, with the global variant expected to feature OxygenOS on Android 15.
### Advanced Camera System and Battery Life
The OnePlus 13 maintains a harmonious rear camera setup with a primary, ultrawide, and telephoto configuration. All three sensors are optimized by Hasselblad, ensuring high-quality imaging. The main camera is Sony’s LYT 808 with OIS, the 3x periscope is the LYT 600 (also with OIS), and the ultrawide is Samsung’s JN5 sensor. The front-facing 32MP camera carries over from the OnePlus 12, featuring a 1/2.74” sensor with an f/2.4 aperture. The device also introduces a Silicon Carbide battery, allowing for a larger 6000mAh cell in a similar footprint. This results in an 11% increase in battery capacity compared to the OnePlus 12. Despite the larger battery, charging speeds remain impressive, with 100W wired, 50W wireless, and 10W reverse wireless charging. The phone can reach 50% in just 13 minutes and 100% in 36 minutes.

## Xiaomi 15 Ultra – Overview
The Xiaomi 15 Ultra is a flagship smartphone that pushes the boundaries of mobile technology with cutting-edge hardware, a premium design, and industry-leading camera capabilities. With a powerful Snapdragon chipset, a high-refresh-rate AMOLED display, and an advanced Leica-powered camera system, this device is designed for users who demand the best in performance, photography, and innovation.
### Design & Build
The Xiaomi 15 Ultra features a glass front, aerospace-grade glass fiber back or eco-leather (silicone polymer) back, and an aluminum frame, ensuring a premium and durable build. It boasts IP68 water and dust resistance, allowing immersion up to 1.5 meters for 30 minutes. The device comes in multiple color options, including Black, White, Silver Chrome, and Green, catering to various style preferences.
### Display & Visuals
Equipped with a 6.73-inch LTPO AMOLED display, the Xiaomi 15 Ultra delivers an ultra-smooth 120Hz refresh rate, Dolby Vision, and HDR10+ for an immersive viewing experience. With a 3200-nit peak brightness and 1440 x 3200 resolution (~522 ppi density), the display is exceptionally sharp and vibrant. Xiaomi Shield Glass 2.0 adds enhanced durability against scratches and drops.
### Performance & Hardware
At its core, the Xiaomi 15 Ultra is powered by the Qualcomm Snapdragon 8 Elite (3nm) chipset, featuring an octa-core CPU with two high-performance Oryon V2 Phoenix L cores (4.32 GHz) and six Oryon V2 Phoenix M cores (3.53 GHz), paired with the Adreno 830 GPU. This ensures blazing-fast speeds for multitasking, gaming, and demanding applications. The phone is available in multiple configurations, including 256GB with 12GB RAM, 512GB with 16GB RAM, and 1TB with 16GB RAM (UFS 4.1 storage) for ultra-fast data access.
### Camera System – Leica Co-Engineered
Xiaomi continues its partnership with Leica, delivering a professional-grade camera experience. The quad-camera setup consists of:
  * 50 MP (wide) – 1.0"-type sensor, f/1.6 aperture, dual-pixel PDAF, OIS
  * 50 MP (telephoto, 3x optical zoom) – 70mm lens, OIS, dual-pixel PDAF
  * 200 MP (periscope telephoto, 4.3x optical zoom) – multi-directional PDAF, OIS
  * 50 MP (ultrawide, 115˚ FOV) – f/2.2 aperture, dual-pixel PDAF
  * TOF 3D sensor (depth)


The laser autofocus, color spectrum sensor, and Leica lenses further enhance image quality. It supports 8K@30fps video recording, 4K@120fps, and 1080p up to 1920fps slow motion, with Dolby Vision HDR 10-bit recording.
On the front, the 32 MP selfie camera captures detailed shots with 4K@60fps video support and gyro-EIS stabilization.
### Battery & Charging
The 5410 mAh Silicon-Carbon Li-Ion battery ensures all-day endurance. It supports 90W wired charging (PD3.0, QC3+), 80W wireless charging, and 10W reverse wireless charging, making it one of the fastest-charging flagships on the market.
### Connectivity & Features
The device is equipped with Wi-Fi 7, Bluetooth 6.0, dual-SIM + eSIM support, 5G connectivity, and USB Type-C 3.2 Gen 2 with DisplayPort support. It also features an infrared port for remote control functionality. The under-display ultrasonic fingerprint sensor ensures fast and secure authentication, while two-way satellite communication provides emergency connectivity in remote locations.

### Conclusion
The Xiaomi 15 Ultra is a powerhouse flagship that excels in every aspect—from its stunning AMOLED display and top-tier Snapdragon 8 Elite processor to its industry-leading Leica camera system and ultra-fast charging capabilities. Designed for power users, mobile photographers, and tech enthusiasts, this device sets a new benchmark in premium smartphone innovation.

## Samsung Galaxy Z Fold 6: A Refined Foldable Experience
#### Design and Display
The Samsung Galaxy Z Fold 6 introduces a refined design with a more boxy approach, making it slightly shorter and wider than its predecessor. This new design also includes a larger vapor chamber for better heat dissipation. The device is lighter, weighing just 239 grams, making it comparable to regular flagships. The Z Fold 6 has earned an IP48 rating, making it more resistant to dust and debris compared to the IPX8 rating of the Fold 5. The outer display is now 6.3 inches diagonally with an aspect ratio of 22.1:9, while the inner 7.6-inch Infinity Flex screen has a 20.9:18 aspect ratio. Both screens feature an adaptive refresh rate from 1-120Hz, with the cover display protected by Corning’s Gorilla Glass 2.
#### Performance and Software
Powered by the Qualcomm Snapdragon 8 Gen 3 chip, optimized specifically for Galaxy phones, the Z Fold 6 offers top-tier performance. It comes with 12GB of LPDDR5X RAM and storage options of 256GB, 512GB, and 1TB (UFS 4.0). The device runs on One UI 6.1.1 based on Android 14, with Samsung promising seven years of OS upgrades. Galaxy AI is a standout feature, offering innovative tools like Circle to Search, Interpreter for real-time translation, Note Assist for summarizing notes, and Sketch to Image, which transforms sketches into realistic images.
#### Camera and Battery
The Z Fold 6 features a comprehensive camera setup with a 50MP primary camera with OIS and 2x optical zoom, a 10MP telephoto with 3x optical zoom, and a 12MP ultrawide camera with an f/2.2 aperture and 123º field of view. There’s also a 10MP selfie camera on the cover screen and a 4MP under-display camera. The device is equipped with a 4,400mAh battery, supporting 25W fast charging, 15W wireless charging, and 4.5W reverse wireless charging. While the battery capacity is modest, it offers all-day battery life, even with heavy use.
### Conclusion
The Samsung Galaxy Z Fold 6 is a refined and powerful foldable smartphone. With its improved design, high-performance hardware, and innovative AI features, it offers a premium experience. Despite minor changes in camera hardware, the overall package makes it a compelling choice for those seeking the best in foldable technology.

## Phantom V Fold 2 Overview
### Design and Display
The Phantom V Fold 2 maintains its 7.85-inch inner screen and 6.42-inch cover display from its predecessor. A notable improvement is its slimmer design, measuring 6.1 mm when unfolded and 12 mm when folded, while the weight has been reduced to 249 grams, down from nearly 300 grams.
### Performance
It is powered by the MediaTek Dimensity 9000+ chipset. Despite being lighter, the device houses a larger battery, with a 5,750 mAh capacity. It supports 70W wired charging and 15W wireless charging. The phone comes with 12 GB of physical RAM and 12 GB of extended RAM, providing 24 GB RAM. It also offers 512 GB of internal storage.
### AI Features
Tecno has integrated the Ella AI assistant, powered by Google Gemini, into the Phantom V Fold 2. This assistant offers several functionalities, including Smart Q&A for real-time answers, AI Summary for summarizing PDFs and webpages, and AI Translation, which provides live translations during calls. Additionally, the AI suite includes AI Writing for tasks like proofreading and text generation.
Other AI-driven features, such as AI Artboard for transforming scribbles into drawings and AI Wallpaper, allow users to create custom wallpapers using text prompts.
### Camera 
The Phantom V Fold 2’s camera has three 50 MP sensors for wide, ultra-wide, and portrait shots. The device also features two 32 MP selfie cameras, one on the cover screen and another on the inner display. To continue with the AI in the camera department, Tecno’s Universal Tone Technology enhances photo quality by accurately capturing diverse skin tones.

## Samsung Galaxy S25 Ultra Overview
### Display and Design
The Galaxy S25 Ultra has a 6.9-inch QHD+ LTPO screen with a refresh rate of 1-120 Hz, which is a little larger than the S24 Ultra's. Clarity is guaranteed even in bright outdoor conditions because to its max brightness of 2600 nits.
In terms of design, Samsung has now eschewed the traditional boxy appearance in favor of more softened corners. Here, Corning Gorilla Armor 2 is utilized on the front and back, with titanium frames sandwiched between. In the meanwhile, the phone comes in a variety of titanium-inspired color variants, including as Gray, Silver Blue, White Silver, and Black. In a similar vein, the phone weighs 218 grams and is 8.2 mm thick, which is significantly less than its predecessor, the S24 Ultra, which weighed 232 grams.
### Camera system
A 50MP telephoto lens with 5x optical zoom, a 10MP telephoto lens with 3x zoom, a 50MP ultrawide lens, and a 200MP wide camera are all features of the smartphone. It also has a 12MP wide-angle front camera for video calls and selfies. The phone now has LOG mode, which allows you to record videos professionally and elevate them to a far better degree of post-production. It can capture videos in up to 8K at 30 frames per second and 4K at 60 frames per second.
### Performance and Battery
The Snapdragon 8 Elite for Galaxy CPU powers the Galaxy S25 Ultra, which is designed for intense gaming and multitasking. It has up to 1TB of UFS 4.0 storage and up to 16GB of LPDDR5X RAM. It also has a 5000 mAh battery that can be charged using 45W wired, 15W wireless, and 4.5W reverse wireless.
### Software and Updates
Up to seven years of software updates are promised for the phone, which runs One UI 7. It presents a new "Galaxy AI" platform while keeping AI characteristics from its predecessors. Personalized suggestions, conversational search, and "Circle to Search," which can identify sounds, are just a few of the capabilities that Galaxy AI provides. Additionally, the most recent S25 Ultra supports Gemini 2.0, which was created in collaboration with Google and adds a touch of Google's distinctive ideas to improve the user experience.

## Vivo X200 Pro Overview
### Design and Display
Speaking of the design, the Vivo X200 Pro boasts a curved frame design with a glossy back and an Oreo-styled circular camera module on the rear. It is available in four color options: Cosmos Black, and Titanium Grey. In terms of ingress protection, it secures both IP68 + IP69 ratings against dust and water damage.
Upfront, the curved screen has bid a farewell but not completely, if you take a closer look. The Vivo X200 Pro now sports a flat display with lightly curved edges on all four corners, like on the Xiaomi 14 Pro. It is a 6.78-inch AMOLED panel with 2K resolution and a 120Hz refresh rate.
### Zeiss coated cameras
The star of the show to no one’s surprise, the mighty Zeiss cameras here backed up by Vivo’s custom V3+ imaging chip on the Vivo X200 Pro. And the most interesting among the pack is the Zeiss 200MP APO Super Telephoto lens with a 1/1.4-inch sensor size and Zeiss’s superior chromatic control, ensuring superb clarity and accurate colors. It now offers up to 135mm portraits which is like a 5.5X zoom. At the same time, the optical zoom quality is 3.7X (85mm).
Likewise, the main camera is a 1/1.28-inch 50MP Sony LYT-818 sensor with Vivo’s self-developed blueprint sensor technology, improving ghosting and stray light effects to form a realistic output. Lastly, there is a 50MP ultrawide unit with Autofocus and 119˚FoV and a 32MP selfie snapper. Moreover, the Vivo X200 Pro can capture up to 8K res videos at 30fps from the rear camera and up to 4K 60fps videos from the front camera.
### 3nm Processor
Powering the core is a Mediatek Dimesnity 9400 processor, a 3nm fabbed flagship chip. It features a core Cortex-X925 at 3.63GHz, three Cortex-X4 cores at 3.3 GHz, and four Cortex-A720 cores at 2.4GHz. Meanwhile, the Immortalis-G925 GPU handles the graphics. Vivo has paired the chip with up to 16GB of RAM and 1TB of UFS 4.0 storage. Likewise, the Vivo X200 Pro boots on OriginOS 5.0 built on top of Android 15.
### Battery and Others
Moving on, the Vivo X200 Pro gets its juice from a sizeable 6000mAh high-density Silicon Carbon battery with 90W wired fast charging support, 30W wireless, and reverse wired charging support. Connectivity features include 5G, WiFi 7, Bluetooth 5.4, GPS, NFC, Infrared, and a USB Type-C 3.2 port.

## Vivo Y03 Overview
The Vivo Y03 is a budget-friendly smartphone that offers exceptional value without compromising on performance. With its stylish design, reliable features, and affordable price, this device is perfect for those seeking a practical and efficient companion.
### Display and Design
A 6.56-inch LCD touchscreen display with 720 x 1612 pixels and a smooth refresh rate of 90 Hz is a feature of the Vivo Y03. Additionally, it is available in two stylish colors: Gem Green and Space Black. 
### Performance and Storage
MediaTek's Helio G85 SoC powers the Vivo Y03's internal components, which should provide respectable performance for daily duties. Even though it lacks 5G connectivity, it ought still meet all of your standard smartphone requirements. It also runs Funtouch OS 14 on top of Android 14, which offers the newest features and improvements.  
  
You'll have enough room for your movies and programs with 4GB of LPDDR4x RAM and 64GB or 128GB of storage. Additionally, a 4GB RAM extension is supported. In Nepal, only the 4/64GB trim is currently offered.
### Cameras
For more imaginative photos, the Vivo Y03 has a QVGA decorative camera in addition to its 13 MP primary back camera. A 5 MP front camera is also included for taking fast selfies or making video calls.
### Battery and Extras
The Vivo Y03 boasts a powerful 5,000 mAh battery that should last you the entire day. A 15W wired charging connector is available for charging the Vivo Y03. Additionally, it has IP54 certification for protection to dust and splashes.

## Tecno Spark 30C Overview
### Design and Display
The Tecno Spark 30C looks pretty standard for a smartphone. There isn’t much going on over here, it has a large centre-aligned camera island. It is IP54-rated and is available in three outlooks: Orbit Black, Orbit White, and Magic Skin 3.0. The former has a monotone finish, while the middle option has a bit of gradient to it. The latter choice stands out the most, as it has vegan leather for its back panel.
The display is also a standard game. It has a 6.67-inch screen, however, the panel type has not been specified by the company. It is likely an LCD, as it is the most sensible option. Regardless, the Tecno Spark 30C offers you an HD+ resolution and a smooth refresh rate of 120Hz. It also supports touch inputs even when the screen has water or oil on it.
### Performance
Under the helm is the MediaTek Helio G81 chipset, which launched near the end of August. Even though it has been a while since it was launched, MediaTek still has not listed it on its website. This is why, we are taking Nanoreview as a reference for the information on the SoC. As per them, the silicon comes with eight cores, 12nm fabrication, and a peal clock speed of 2.0GHz. While the Redmi 14C did feature the Helio G81 Ultra, the Tecno Spark 30C is likely the first phone to have the standard version.
This smartphone comes in three memory choices: 4GB, 6GB, and 8GB. Meanwhile, you can choose between 128GB and 256GB for the internal storage. Altogether, the Tecno Spark 30C is available in four configurations: 4GB + 128GB, 4GB + 256GB, 6GB + 128GB, and 8GB + 256GB. Users can virtually double the memory on this thing, however, it appears there is no option for storage expansion. Talking of the software, this phone boots on Android 14.
### Camera and the rest
In terms of the camera, you get a primary 50MP unit at the back. It is assisted by a dummy lens, making it look like a dual-camera setup. However, that is definitely not the case. Likewise, it has a decent 8MP shooter on the front. In the tank, Tecno Spark 30C packs a 5,000mAh battery with 18W fast charging support. It has a stereo speaker setup with DTS tuning and apparently can deliver up to 300% louder volume. Lastly, the phone is equipped with an IR blaster too.

## Vivo Y18: A Budget-Friendly Option
The Vivo Y18 is a mid-range smartphone that offers a premium design and notable features at an affordable price. It comes in two stylish colors: Mocha Brown and Wave Aqua, with an IP54 rating for dust and splash resistance. The device also features a side-mounted fingerprint sensor integrated into the power button for convenient and secure access.
One of the standout features of the Y18 is its display. It boasts a 6.56-inch LCD screen with a 90Hz refresh rate, providing smooth visuals. The resolution is 720 x 1612 pixels, and the display is certified for genuine eye protection by TUV. In High Brightness Mode, the screen reaches up to 840 nits, making it one of the brightest in its segment.
The camera setup includes a 50MP main rear sensor, complemented by an 8MP front camera for selfies and videos. While the secondary rear camera is only 0.08MP, the main sensor should deliver decent photos in various lighting conditions.
Under the hood, the Vivo Y18 is powered by the MediaTek Helio G85 SoC, paired with 6GB of RAM. It offers 128GB of internal storage, which can be expanded via a microSD card. The device runs on Android 14 with Vivo’s Funtouch OS 14, providing a smooth and user-friendly experience.
The Y18 is equipped with a 5,000mAh battery that supports 15W wired charging, ensuring long-lasting power for daily use. Overall, the Vivo Y18 is a well-rounded device that balances design, display quality, and performance, making it a solid choice for those seeking a reliable smartphone without breaking the bank.

## OPPO A60 Overview
### Design and Display
The OPPO A60 comes in a flat design and a pill-shaped camera island on the back. It is available in two different finishes — the first one is a monotone Midnight Purple, while the other is ripple-patterned Ripple Blue. It also comes with IP54 water and dust resistance along with MIL-STD-810H certification.
On the front, you get a 6.67-inch A-Si LCD panel with KK6 cover glass. The screen stretches HD+ in resolution and offers a refresh rate of 90Hz. Additionally, it comes with a maximum touch sampling rate of 240Hz, a peak brightness of 950nits, and an 83% [NTSC](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NTSC) colour gamut.
### Performance
For the primary performance, the OPPO A60 relies on the Qualcomm Snapdragon 680 chipset. It is a 4G-only chip that comes with eight cores, 6nm fabrication, and a peak clock speed of 2.4GHz. Moreover, the chip is about three years old at this point and prioritizes battery life more than anything else.
Other than that, you get an 8GB LPDDR4x RAM coupled with two options of UFS 2.2 storage. The storage option includes 128GB or 256GB internal and support for expansion via a MicroSD card. Similarly, it allows you to double the RAM capacity virtually if you require more memory on your phone. On the software front, the OPPO A60 boots on ColorOS 14.0.1 based on Android 14.
### Camera and the rest
Moving on to the imaging capabilities of this phone, it wields a dual camera setup on the back. The primary of which is a 50MP shooter while the secondary camera is a measly 2MP unit. On the other hand, you get an 8MP selfie camera on the OPPO A60.
In the tank, the phone comes with a 5,000 mAh cell with 45W SUPERVOOC charging support. For security, you get a side-mounted fingerprint reader as well as a facial recognition feature. Meanwhile, the OPPO A60 offers wireless connectivity through dual SIM, 4G cellular, dual-band WiFi, Bluetooth v5.0, and NFC (region-specific) support. Likewise, the wired connections on this phone are handled by a USB Type-C port and a 3.5mm headphone jack.

## OPPO Reno 12 F (4G) Overview:
### Design and Display
The OPPO Reno 12 F features a sleek design with a flat frame and a hole-punch cutout display. The rear panel has a glossy finish in Olive Green and an attractive wave-like pattern in Amber Orange. The circular camera module is highlighted with a Halo Light, known as the Cosmos Ring design, inspired by luxury watches. The device is IP64 rated for dust and water resistance. The front houses a 6.67-inch OLED display with a 120Hz refresh rate and FHD+ resolution, protected by AGC DT-Star2 glass. The wet touch feature allows usage even with wet hands.
### Performance
Powered by the Snapdragon 685 SoC, the OPPO Reno 12 F is built on a 6nm process with four Cortex-A73 cores at 2.8GHz and four Cortex-A53 cores at 1.9GHz. The Adreno 610 GPU handles graphics. The device comes with 8GB of RAM and up to 512GB of internal storage, running on ColorOS 14.1 based on Android 14.
### AI Features
The Reno 12 F boasts AI Eraser 2.0 for removing unwanted objects in the background and AI LinkBoost for stable connections in weak network areas, thanks to its 360-degree antenna design. The BeaconLink feature allows Bluetooth-based calls within 200 meters without a mobile signal or internet.
### Camera and Battery
The triple-camera setup includes a 50MP primary shooter, an 8MP ultrawide lens (112° FOV), and a 2MP macro unit. The front features a 32MP camera for selfies and video calls. The device is powered by a 5000mAh battery with 45W fast charging support. Connectivity options include 5G, WiFi 5, Bluetooth 5.3, GPS, NFC, and a USB Type-C port. An in-display fingerprint scanner ensures biometric security.
The OPPO Reno 12 F (4G) combines a stylish design, high-quality display, robust performance, and advanced AI features, making it a compelling choice in the mid-range segment.

## OPPO Reno 11 F 5G Overview
### Design and Display
The phone comes in a flat boxy design with an IP65 rating and a large rectangular camera island. Additionally, there are two circular cutouts for the cameras that house three lenses. All this makes the rear panel of the phone very eye-catching. The OPPO Reno 11 F 5G is available in three colours: Palm Green, Ocean Blue, and Coral Purple. The first, and the last option come in a glittery finish while the middle one flaunts water-like patterns on the back.
On the front, you are greeted with a 2.5D curved screen that measures 6.7 inches diagonally. The panel here is an OLED that is twice-reinforced by Panda glass. Meanwhile, the screen spans FHD+ in resolution with 1,080 horizontal and 2,412 vertical pixels. It also offers a refresh rate of 120Hz, maximum touch sampling rate of 240Hz, and peak brightness of 1,100 nits. Other than that, it supports a 100% DCI-P3 colour gamut.
### Performance
For its primary performance, the OPPO Reno 11 F 5G relies on the MediaTek Dimensity 7050 chipset. This is a 2023 processor that comes with eight cores, 6 nanometre fabrication, and a peak clock speed of 2,600 MHz. Meanwhile, the graphics on this phone are handled by ARM Mali-G68 MC4.
The silicone is then coupled with an LPDDR4x-4266MHz RAM and UFS3.1 storage. This phone only comes in a single 8GB + 256GB configuration. However, it does offer RAM extension and storage expansion of 8GB, and 2TB via a MicroSD card respectively. In the meantime, this phone boots on the ColorOS 14.0 based on Android 14.
### Camera and the rest
A 64MP primary shooter with autofocus support spearheads the camera department on this phone. Furthermore, an 8MP ultrawide camera with 112° FOV as well as a 2MP macro lens further assist the primary shooter. On the other hand, you have a 32MP snapper sitting underneath a centre-aligned hole-punch camera.
The OPPO Reno 11 F 5G draws its power from a 5,000 mAh battery while supporting 67W SUPERVOOC charging. For wireless connectivity, you get dual SIM with 5G cellular support. In addition to that, this also comes with dual-band WiFi 6, Bluetooth 5.2, and NFC capabilities. Meanwhile, for the wired connection, you have to make do with a single USB Type-C port.

## Redmi A5 4G 
### Display and Design
The device features a 6.88-inch 120Hz LCD display, likely with 720p+ resolution. Additionally, it comes in four color options and includes a side-mounted fingerprint sensor for quick access.
### Camera Setup
The Redmi A5 4G sports an 8MP front camera, upgraded from the 5MP in previous models. However, the rear camera has been downgraded to 32MP from the 50MP sensors found in earlier versions.
### Performance
The phone runs on a Unisoc T7250 chipset with 4G connectivity. This processor contains two Cortex-A75 cores at 1.8GHz and six Cortex-A55 cores at 1.6GHz, paired with a Mali-G57 GPU running at 850MHz. Performance-wise, it’s similar to the Helio G81 Ultra in the Redmi A3 Pro but weaker than the Snapdragon 4s Gen 2 found in the Redmi A4.
### Battery
The Redmi A5 4G is powered by a 5,200mAh battery with 18W charging support, though the package includes a 15W adapter.

## Tecno Spark Go 2024 Overview:
### Design and Display
The Tecno Spark Go 2024 features a sleek design with a glass front, plastic back, and frame, ensuring durability without sacrificing aesthetics. Additionally, Its 6.6-inch IPS LCD with a 90Hz refresh rate provides a smooth viewing experience, making it suitable for multimedia consumption and everyday tasks.
### Performance and Software
Powered by Android 13 (Go edition) with HIOS 13 overlay, the Spark Go 2024 runs efficiently on the Unisoc T606 chipset. Although not designed for gaming or demanding applications, the octa-core CPU ensures smooth multitasking, the phone is offered with 4 GB RAM and 64 GB Storage with 4 GB virtual expansion.
### Camera 
Equipped with a modest 13MP primary camera and an auxiliary lens, the Tecno Spark Go 2024 delivers satisfactory photography capabilities, complemented by features like dual-LED flash and HDR support. In addition, the 8MP front camera with dual-LED flash facilitates decent selfie-taking even in low-light conditions.
### Battery and Connectivity
One of the standout features of the Tecno Spark Go 2024 is its impressive 5000mAh battery, providing extended usage without frequent recharges. Furthermore, the inclusion of a USB Type-C port with 10W wired charging ensures convenient and efficient power replenishment. Additionally, the device supports essential connectivity options such as Wi-Fi, Bluetooth, GPS, and FM radio.

# Infinix Smart 9 Overview:
## Design and Display
The Infinix Smart 9 features a standard design with flat edges and a frame, a squircle camera island, and a grainy finish on the back. It has a better-fleshed-out appearance than its predecessor, the Infinix Smart 8, and enjoys an IP54 rating for dust and splash resistance. The device is available in Metallic Black, Neo Titanium, Mint Green, and Sandstone Gold color options. The phone has a 6.7-inch IPS a-Si LCD panel with HD+ resolution (720 x 1600 pixels) and a refresh rate of up to 120Hz, offering a typical brightness of 500 nits. The screen also maintains responsiveness even when used with wet and greasy hands.
## Performance
The Infinix Smart 9 is powered by the MediaTek Helio G81 processor, an octa-core chipset with 2x Cortex-A75 cores at 2.0 GHz and 6x Cortex-A55 cores at 1.7 GHz, paired with Mali-G52 MC2 GPU. The device comes with either 3GB or 4GB of RAM, which can be doubled through software means. Storage options include 64GB or 128GB, with support for external expansion up to 2TB via a MicroSD card. The phone runs on XOS 14.0, based on Android 14 (Go Edition).
## Camera and Battery
The rear camera setup includes a 13MP primary shooter coupled with an undisclosed auxiliary unit. The front features an 8MP snapper for selfies and face scanning. The Infinix Smart 9 is equipped with a 5000mAh non-removable battery, supporting 10W wired charging. The phone also includes dual speakers with DTS sound, clear dialogue, and a headphone jack.
## Conclusion
The Infinix Smart 9 offers a balanced combination of a large display, decent performance, and essential features at an affordable price point. With its 120Hz refresh rate and expandable storage, it caters to users seeking a reliable entry-level smartphone.

## Redmi A3 Overview
The Redmi A3 is a budget-friendly smartphone that offers exceptional value without compromising on performance. With its stylish design, powerful features, and affordable price, this device is perfect for those seeking a reliable and efficient companion.
### Design and Display
To begin with, the Redmi A3's construction includes a glass front body, a glass back, and a plastic frame. A dual camera arrangement is housed in a striking circular camera module on the back of this smartphone. A 6.71-inch LCD screen with HD+ resolution and a refresh rate of 90 Hz is included up front. Even though it's a low-cost phone, the screen is protected by Gorilla Glass 3.
### Performance
The MediaTek Helio G36 chipset powers the smartphone's internal components. Four Cortex-A53 cores operating at 2.2GHz and four clocking at 1.6GHz are present in this 12nm fabbed octa-core processor. The PowerVR GE8320 GPU is in charge of the graphics tasks. Similarly, Redmi has combined this CPU with 128GB of eMMC 5.1 internal storage and up to 6GB of RAM.
In terms of software, the vanilla Android 14 is different from the MIUI that is typically seen on other Redmi phones. Because it's a low-cost phone and because the Redmi A1 and A2 have the same close-to-stock Android OS, it makes sense.
### Camera
In terms of optics, the gadget has two cameras. An 8MP camera and a pointless 0.08MP auxiliary lens are its main features. The U-shaped notch has a 5MP camera for video calls and selfies. Both cameras are capable of producing 1080p films at 30 frames per second.
### Battery and Others
The Redmi A3 is powered by a 5000mAh battery that supports 10W wired charging. WiFi, 4G, Bluetooth 5.3, a 3.5mm headphone socket, and a USB Type-C 2.0 port (for the first time on a Redmi A-Series smartphone) are among the connectivity choices available here. Additionally, a fingerprint scanner is positioned on the side for biometric security.
